################################
1. Introduction [Intro]
################################


********************************
1.1. Game Info                  
********************************

This game was released on
November 18th in the USA and it
is a sequel to the previous Rune
Factory - A Fantasy Harvest
Moon. The story of this game is
not directly connected to the
previous one, so even if you
didn't play the first you can
still enjoy this game the same
way.

For the ones who don't know
about this game, it's pretty
much the same as the previous
Harvest Moon series except that
now, besides taking care of a
farm you also need to explore
dungeons, fight monsters and
level up, that is, now some RPG
features were added to increase
the variety of tasks you can
perform.

Some improvements were made to
the previous controls, mainly
about the touch screen so it is
a bit more functional. A major
difference in this game to the
previous Rune Factory is that
now you're able to play with two
generations of characters
because, once you get married
and raise your baby, the main
focus of the game will be
transfered to your child, so
he'll have to take care of the
farm instead of his dad. It is
here that you can say the game
really shows everything it has,
since there are a lot of things
you couldn't do before and now
will be available.

If you think it is interesting
to take care of a farm and deal
with monsters and quests or if
you always liked Harvest Moon or
liked the previous Rune Factory,
you should really try this game.


********************************
1.2. About Authors [Authors]
********************************

Hello, we're Lerion and Winchu.
This is our first time writing a
FAQ, so if you see something
wrong or if you want to suggest
improvements, feel free to
contact us via email:
lerionfaqs@gmail.com

Even though the e-mail is on
Lerion's name, both of us can be
contacted by this account as
well as we both can also answer
the new mails.

We started writing this guide
for ourselves, since there was
none at the time and we needed
some data for later
consultation. But after start
writing it, we thought it would
be nice if we could share with
the others, so we started to
format it like a FAQ so we could
submit it later if possible.

We're not a native American or
anything so it's possible that
this guide contains some
misspelling / grammatical
mistakes, so we apologize. If
you see mistakes in this text
and want to help to correct them
you can also contact us to alert
about them.

1.3 Guide Info                  
********************************

The update has finally come, now
the guide covers both
generations and I can say it's
finished, except for some
possible mistakes there might be
or some improvements that can be
made later to enrich the guide
even more. I must say the second
part of the guide was mainly
(near totally) written by
Winchu, so all the credits for
this part must be given to him,
as all I did was to support him
a bit in the end and revise the
text before publishing.

The info displayed in this guide
was based in my, and my
collaborators, experience of the
game, so it's possible some
things will be missing, even
though we tried to cover
everything we found in the game.
If you see a hole or if
something said in this guide is
not correct you can also contact
me to alert me about it if you
want.

I wanted to make a guide easier
to read, visually speaking, so I
used different characters and
symbols for the header and the
tables, trying to make it easier
to identify each component. So,
just to make things clearer,
here's an explanation on the
notation and features of this
guide:

- Double reference: Both numbers

Still speaking about the tables,
each even item has a line of .
(dots) connecting the columns.
That was made in order to try to
make easier to read, as I
usually get lost trying to
follow blank lines.

The ones who seek quick info
without details, can take a look
at the section "Quicklists"
where I created sections of some
things that can be interesting
to have a quick look sometimes
but are scattered in the middle
of a lot of text in the main
body of the guide.

Notice that tables that are
already "clean" in the main

quicklist section, such as the

################################
2. Game Basics [Basics]
################################

This section will cover the
basics of this game, hence the
title. Here I'll explain a bit
about the game commands, what
you can do and some of the main
changes I noticed from the first
game.


********************************
2.1. First Steps [Steps]
********************************

For the ones who not aware, this
game is basically a farm
simulator with some RPG-like
features, such as entering
dungeons, fighting and capturing
monsters.

Your main objectives in this
game will be to keep a good farm
and a good life. That is, you'll
have to keep an active farm,
growing crops, animals, etc.
while trying to be friends with
the villagers and eventually
getting married with one of the
girls available.

That said, I'll first explain a
bit about how you move around in
the game and do some tasks using
the controls. First I'll tell
about the basic controls and
then about how to use the touch
screen controls.


================================
2.1.1. Basic Controls [Controls]
================================

Here's what each button will do
once pressed and some
combination of buttons you need
to know. Notice that these
commands assume your using the
default button configuration of
the game. If you already changed
them in the Settings menu, just
invert the L and R buttons
explanation if you switched
them. The same applies to the
D-Pad and the ABXY buttons.

So here's the explanation:

now you can do a lot of thing.
You can even play the game
completely by using only the
touch screen if you want, even
though I still prefer to use the
buttons in general.

********************************
2.2. Your House                 
********************************

In this section you'll know a
little more about your own
house. I'll try to give a brief
explanation about the furniture
you can interact with in your
place. You can interact with
them by getting close to one of
them and pressing the action
button or touching the screen.

I'll start from the one in the
upper left corner and proceed to
the right until the wall and
then I'll go back to the left
again and go down. So here's the
list:

First Floor
--------------------------------
Diary: Allows you to save the
game any time you want. Shelf:
You can store non-eatable items
you don't use frequently here.
Refrigerator: You can store food
and alike here. Chest: No use
for it yet. Only in the
beginning of the second
generation. The
    old tools from Kyle will be 
Fireplace: No use as well.
Bookshelf: Presents a tutorial
about fighting.


Second Floor
--------------------------------
Calendar: It's on the right
corner. Shows the calendar and
the festivals days.
    Also, every time someone tel
    here right away.
Mirror: It's on the vanity table
in the left bedroom. Allows you
to exchange
    items with other people eith
    (Wi-Fi Connection).
Double Bed: It's in the left
bedroom. Allows you to sleep and
call a day. This
    way you'll replenish your HP
    up on the next day.
Single Bed: It's on right
bedroom. Works the same way as
the Double Bed. Diary: Allows
you to save the game any time
you want.


********************************
2.3. Sleeping Time [Sleep]
********************************

The time you go to bed and sleep
affects your status the next
day. That is, only if you're an
extreme player. See below how
much of the total HP and RP you
restore and what else changes
depending on the time you sleep
(when I say "until time", I mean
not including that time, for
example, if I say "until AM
1:00", that means that'll happen
if you go to bed before AM 1:00
or until AM 12:59. If you go to
bed at AM 1:00 or AM 1:01 and so
on, it'll be the same as going
to bed until AM 2:00):

- Until AM 1:00: 100% HP & RP, d
- Until AM 2:00: 100% HP & RP, d
- Until AM 3:00: 80% HP & RP, do
- Until AM 4:00: 50% HP & RP, ge
- Until AM 5:00: 50% HP & RP, ge
- AM 5:00: The character automat
 wakes up at AM 10:00. If he's i
 if he's in a dungeon, he'll wak

* If you're wondering what does 
Ailments subsection in the
Fighting section.


********************************
2.4. Weather                    
********************************

It is important to know about
the weather when farming, as
these may affect your activities
of the day. Notice that even
though it doesn't seem so, the
dungeons are also affected by
weather changes. I'll present
some of the consequences of each
different weather below:

- Hurricane: You can't go out of
 destroys some of the crops you 
- Rainy: Changes the schedule of
 of the fields.
- Snow Storm:  The same as Hurri
- Snowy: The same as Rainy, but 
- Sunny: Usual weather, doesn't 

If you want to know about the
weather forecast for 1 day, you
can ask Alicia to tell you by
paying 10G. You can also ask her
to change the weather if, for
example, you know a hurricane
will come and you don't want it.
You can choose one of two
possible weathers: sunny (pay
100G in first generation and
200G in second) or rainy (1000G
in first and 2000G in second).


********************************
2.5. Lost and Found [Lost]
********************************

In the first floor of Byron's
(the mayor's) house you'll find
a box (in front of the entrance
door, in the wall) that will
hold any important item you
accidentally toss out. So, if
you ever throw away an
irreplaceable item, such as a
proposal item or anything like
that, you don't need to panic.
Just proceed to Byron's house
and check the box and most
likely the item will be there.
If not, that means you can
obtain it again by some other
way. Notice that if you lose a
quest item you don't need to
look for it in the Lost and
Found box, you can go to the
bulletin board, cancel the quest
and start it again.


################################
3. Start Menu                   
################################

Here I'll explain a bit about
the info you can see in the
Start Menu (the one you can see
when you press the Start
button). There are six menus
listed in the top of the screen
as well as a close button at the
extreme right (the X icon). So
here's an explanation about each
of them:


********************************
3.1. Inventory/Status
     [Inventory]
********************************

The first menu you'll see when
you open the Start Menu. In this
one you can see the status of
your character in the upper
screen and his inventory in the
lower screen.

About the status: The left table
shows you from top to bottom:
the name of your character, his
level, the amount of experience
needed to level up again (this
bar fills up as you fight and
defeat monsters and, when it's
finally full you level up).
Below the "Next" bar there are
the HP and RP bars and your
money.

Concerning the HP bar: The HP
(Health Points) bar represents
your physical condition. This
bar will go down every time
you're hurt by a monster of when
you try to use a tool after you
have already depleted the RP
bar. If the HP bar empties
you'll faint and, if you're in
the village when that happens
you'll wake up on the clinic and
lose the day. On the other hand,
if that happens when you're in a
dungeon, there won't be anyone
around to rescue you when you
faint, so instead of being
carried over to the clinic
you'll actually die and you'll
have to load the game from where
you last saved it, so be
EXTREMELY careful about your HP
when you're inside a dungeon.
You can restore a bit of HP by
eating some grasses or crops, by
drinking a potion, by taking a
shower in the bathhouse of the
village, using spells or by
activating some special slabs in
the dungeons.

Concerning the RP bar: RP stands
to Rune Points. This bar
represents both your stamina and
your magical energy. Every time
you use a tool, swing a weapon
or use a Rune Ability this bar
will go down a bit. If you
deplete your RP you won't be
able to use Rune Abilities
anymore, but you'll still be
able to use tools and weapons
consuming the HP bar instead of
the RP one every time. To
restore RP, you need to collect
the runes generated by grown
crops (recover 50 RP) or the
flowers (recover 12 RP) and
crystals (recover 24 RP) in the
dungeons, eat some specific
foods or take a shower (recover
100 RP) in the bathhouse of the
village.

Well, let's go back to the upper
status screen, now I'll tell
about the right table: This
table shows the attribute values
of your character. These values
go up as you level up and they
affect mainly your fighting
(notice your total HP also grows
up as you level up, but the RP
is always the same).

The last thing about the upper
screen is a bar that I'll call
"Time Bar". This bar is the one
that is shown in this same place
when you're out of the Start
Menu. The Time Bar shows you
from left to right: The
currently year, season, day of
the month and of the week, the
time and lastly the weather.

Now let's turn our attention to
the lower screen, the inventory:
Again there are two tables. The
left one shows your equipped
stuff, that is, what you're
currently wearing or holding.
One item can be placed on each
of the boxes, but you cannot
place anything anywhere, each of
them only accepts proper items
for that place. So here's an
explanation about them:

The top square, the Held box,
holds the item you're currently
holding in your hands. So if you
just picked something up you
should see it in this box. The
same way, if you want to put
something in your hands, you can
just put it in this box.

Next comes the R. Hand (Right
Hand) box. This one will have
the current tool or weapon
you're holding, the one you can
use by pressing the tools
button.

The L. Hand (Left Hand) box is
where you'll be able to equip
shields to increase your defense
in battle. This is a passive
slot, you can't actually use it
for anything. All you need to do
is to equip it here and receive
the benefits it gives (shield
defense only applies when you're
equipped with a shortsword or a
rod).

The Rune Abl. (Rune Abilities)
has two boxes, meaning you can
equip up to two different Rune
Abilities at the same time. The
one placed in the left box can
be activated by pressing the
first Rune Ability button (Y
button or Left in the D-Pad if
you changed controls) and the in
the right box is activated by
pressing the second Rune Ability
button (X button or Up in the
D-Pad).

The last two boxes are the
accessories you can equip to
receive some bonuses. You can
equip up to two of them and the
bonus given by each accessory
may vary a lot, it can be, for
example: increase defense,
increase resistance to an
attribute, increase status, etc.

Finally, the right table of the
lower (touch) screen shows your
backpack. There are 45 slots
available and each of them can
hold up to 9 units of the same
(notice that they must be of the
same level as well, if you have,
for example, a level 1 Onion and
a level 2 one you can't place
both of them in the same slot).


********************************
3.2. Skill                      
********************************

This menu shows the skill levels
of your character, that is, his
ability level at some specifics
tasks. You can increase your
skill levels by actually
performing the action that
benefits from that skill level,
for example, the Weapons Skill
affects the RP consumption when
fighting, so, if you want to
increase the Weapons Skill level
you need to actually fight with
a weapon. Increasing the skill
levels allows you to receive
some benefits when doing
something that depends on that
skill. In general most of them
decreases the amount of RP you
need to perform an action that
depends on that skill. If that
is not the case, I'll tell in
the description of that skill
what it does instead. Here's a
list of what is affected by each
skill and additional effects
they can have on actions:

- Weapons: This skill is also af
 try to fight with a weapon whos
 you'll consume more RP than the
- Farming: Affects the using of 
- Mining: Affects the using of h
- Pharmacy: Affects the success 
 own. The best medicines require
 successfully.
- Accessories: The same as Pharm
- Camping: Affects the use of sl
- Magic: Affects the use of Rune
- Logging: Affects the use of ax
- Fishing: Affects the use of po
- Forging: The same as Pharmacy,
- Cooking: The same as Pharmacy,
- Communication: Affects the tam


********************************
3.3. Accompanying Monster
     [Accompany]
********************************

Here you'll be able to see the
status of the monster that's
accompanying you at the time, if
any. The lower screen will show
a 3D picture of the monster and
the upper one will shows its
status. Let's see a bit about
the status screen.

There are three windows in this
screen. The top one shows an
icon of the monster, its name on
the right and its current HP
below.

The middle window says the
species of the monster and
displays 10 balls that represent
your Friendship Level with that
monster. As you feed and brush
it everyday you'll increase the
Friendship Level and, by doing
so, you increase its fighting
status as well as its produces
qualities, if it's a Produce-
Type monster.

The last window shows a
description about the monster as
well as its Skill (kind of
attack when battles) and its
attribute (affects the damage
dealt / taken from other
attribute monsters).


********************************
3.4. Friendship [Friendship]
********************************

Display the villagers you know
and their Friendship Level
towards you (maximum 10). The
main list in the lower part
shows the name of the villager,
the Friendship Level of this
villager and the Love Level
(this one only appears for some
specific villagers that you can
engage). Besides the main list,
there are also 5 buttons just
above it that allows you to
change the list view. I'll tell
a bit about them:

From left to right, the first
button (a girl face) allows you
to see the Friendship Level of
the villagers. The second button
(a monster face) allows you to
see the Friendship Level of the
monsters you tamed.

The three button on the right,
instead of change the elements
of the list, allows you to sort
the list by some property.
Notice that when you click the
sorting button once, it'll sort
the name in ascending order (the
button will be pointing
upwards), but if you click this
button once again, the names
will be sorted in descending
order (pointing downwards).

About these three buttons: The
first one (Auto) sorts the names
in a way defined by the game (I
think it's by first meeting
order, but I'm not sure). The
second button (a smile face)
sorts the names by friendship
level. The last button (heart)
sorts the names by love level.

and you can get them by

the second generation part of

important to proceed the main

need to take much care of them
because they don't have any
effect on your character, just
check to know what is missing to

Shows what you can configure in
the game, to make it fit you
better. There are only three
options:

- Display Target Box: If it's tu
 of your character (if you don't
 Basic Controls section in this 
 it's just a shortcut to this fu
- L <-> R Switch Buttons: Switch
- D-Pad <-> ABXY Switch Buttons:

If you want your changes to take
effect you need to hit the Save
button in the lower part of the
screen before going out of the
menu. If you make any changes
but didn't like the results,
just hit the Reset button and
the default configuration will
take place.


################################
4. Farming                      
################################

This is the main part of the
game. So first I'll present a
simple tutorial on what should
you do when you start farming.

First of all you need to clear a
small area in your farming field
outside your house. Notice there
are lines on the ground
delimiting 3x3 squares, so try
to clear one of them. If you
still don't have a hammer to
break the big rocks or an axe to
cut the tree stumps, simply pick
and toss the grasses, small
rocks and wooden branches, this
way they'll disappear then you
toss them out and you'll clean a
part of your field.

After doing this, select your
hoe and start tilling the land
you just cleaned, this way
you'll be preparing the field to
plant some seeds on it.

Now select some seeds from your
backpack (if you don't have any,
you can buy them at the general
store or try earn some as a
quest reward or anything), place
yourself in the middle of the
3x3 you tilled and spread the
seeds by pressing the tools
buttons again.

If done correctly, the 9 tilled
soils will have some dots on
them, showing the seeds are
planted. Finally, select your
watering can, refill it if
needed (in the watering pond
near your house) and start
watering all of the seeds on the
ground.

That's it. Now all you have to
do is to water them everyday
until they grow and you can
harvest them to earn some money
and start everything again.

Before someone asks me I'll say
this: even if you forget to
water the crops a day they won't
die, they'll just take a little
longer (1 day in this case) to
grow, so rest at ease.

You can sell your harvested
crops or any valuable item you
want to sell by tossing them in
your shipping box in your farm
(the box just below the water
pond next to your house). Mana
will at PM 3:00 to get the items
from the box and pay you for
them (you don't need to be
around to receive the money). If
you put anything in the box
after PM 3:00, Mana will only
pick and pay for them in the
next day.

After these basics about
farming, I'll tell a bit about
the role of the shipping box
(other than selling), the
farming tools available and
later about the crops you can
grow in the game.


********************************
4.1. The Shipping Box [Shipping]
********************************

Other than selling the items you
throw inside of it, the Shipping
Box also shows you how many of
the possible items you already
sold and how much you earned for
each of them, as well as some
general info about the farm. To
see this info, approach the box
and press the action button or
touch it.

A new menu will open when you do
this. In the lower screen you'll
see a list of the items you
already sold and how much you
earned by selling them until
now. In the upper part of this
screen there are six icons you
can select to change the kind of
items of the list. From left to
right the icons represent:

- Crop Records: Shows info about
 collect from farming soil (gras
- Medicine Records: Info about t
 pharmacies on you own in the se
- Accessory Records: Info about 
 you can only craft them on your
- Cooking Records: Info about th
 able to cook in the second gene
- Fish Records: Info about the f
- Other Records: Info about the 

You can sort the lists in the
same way as you could do in the
Friendship menu (see the Start
Menu section above for more
info).

In the upper screen you can see,
besides the usual description of
the selected item in the lower
part, two tables in the top. The
left table is always fixed, that
is, it doesn't change when you
select another list in the lower
screen. This table shows general
info about your farm: its name,
how much you earned until the
moment (not how much you have,
but the total amount collected
by selling goods without
considering the spendings), the
percentage of the total of
different kinds of items you
already sold at least once and
how much wood and monster feed
you have available.

The right table shows info about
the current list you're looking
at the lower screen. It
contains, the name of the list,
how much you earned until the
moment by selling this kind of
good, the percentage of the
total of that kind of good you
already sold at least once and
finally what item gave the
highest and the lowest income.


********************************
4.2. Farming Tools [Tools]
********************************

In this game, in the first
generation your tools will
already a bit improved, so
you'll be able to use until
level 2 charge from the
beginning.

For the ones who never played a
Harvest Moon game before or
don't know what charge means,
I'll explain about it.

Any tool can be used in
different levels of intensity so
it'll have a different level of
effect when activated. Each of
these levels is what we call a
charge. A level 0 charge is the
standard action you perform when
you simply press the tools
button. If you want to use a
level 1 charge, press and hold
the tools button for a while. If
you do this, you'll see a blue
sphere around the tool you're
using. If you release the button
at this time, the effect of the
tool will be amplified, but
notice you'll also lose more
Rune Point after the action. To
perform a level 2 charge, do the
same as the level 1 charge,
press and hold the tools button.
After a while, the blue sphere
will appear again, but if you do
not release the tools button
just yet and hold it for a
little longer, the sphere will
become purple. Now, if you
release the button during the
purple sphere stage you'll be
able to perform a level 2
charge, that's even more
powerful and also depletes more
of your RP. Notice that, when
using a tool on farming soil,
the area the tool will affect is
marked in red. Most of the time
it'll be a single square, but,
when you charge the hoe or the
watering can, the area will
increase, meaning that, when you
release the charge you'll till
or water, respectively, all of
that area.

Notice that in the first
generation part, the tools will
only be able to charge from
level 0 to level 2, but in the
second generation part of the
game you'll be able to obtain
tools that have even more
charging levels. To activate
them, do the same proceeding,
but hold the button for even
more time and the sphere should
change again, showing that
you'll perform a more powerful
charge.

Also don't forget that once you
enter the second generation part
of the game, all the farming
tools will be rusted. That means
that, besides only being able to
perform a level 0 charge, the
axe and hammer tools won't
cut/break stumps and big rocks
no matter how many times you try
to do destroy them. If you want
to improve your tools, you'll
need to upgrade them in the
Workshop (see Tools Upgrades in
the Forging section for
details).

Below you'll be able to see some
general info about the farming
tools and the effect of the
charge level for each item.

* Second generation only.

********************************
4.3. Crops                      
********************************

In this section you'll find out
about the crops you can plant
and sell to earn some money and
keep your farm. The crops are
organized by the season you can
plant them in. For each of the
crops (or seeds of these crops)
I'll list the seed price at the
general store, how much the seed
is worth for selling (only after
you get the seed maker in the
2nd generation), the crop value
for selling and its growth and
regrowth time.

Also some special seeds can be
only get in second generation
after you find the vegetable
with Inquisitive Waltz in
dungeons and use the Seed Maker
at Alvarna Academy - Workshop.
These seeds will be marked with
* and a small note about where
to find this item will be
available at the table's end.

Now this is something I wanted
to say, but I didn't know
exactly where to place it, so
I'll put it here. Pay attention
when you try to chop the grass
(if you planted it, that is),
because if you accidentally chop
it twice before it regrows,
you'll actually be killing it
and it'll never grow up again,
unless you plant new seeds.

################################
5. Crafting                     
################################

In this section you'll know
about the items you can create
by yourself, either weapons,
tools improvements, cookings and
etc.

Before you start crafting, you
need first to upgrade the
school, asking the mayor to
build the workshop extension.
After it's built, it'll be only
an empty room and you won't be
able to do anything until you
buy from Yue (choose "I want a
bargain.") the proper tools to
start the work (The tools you
need are listed in each
section). Notice Yue doesn't
sell all the items everyday,
each day of the week she'll be
selling a different tool for
crafting, so make sure to go in
the correct date to obtain the
tool (The days of the week are
also mentioned in each section).

You won't be able to craft any
item you want so easily, unless
you have the necessary skill
level to do so. But notice that
even if your skill level is
lower than the minimum skill
level required, you can still
try to craft the item, but
you'll have a lower success rate
of getting a good result. Except
for the cookings, every time you
failure at crafting something
you'll only lose some RP (you
always lose RP when crafting,
even if you get a success) and
you won't obtain any item in the
process (you won't lose the
items you used to try to create
the new item). For cookings this
doesn't apply, as if you try to
cook anything and if it isn't a
success you'll get a "Failed
Dish" as a result and WILL lose
the items you used, so be
careful when cooking.

The success rate when crafting
follows this these rules:

- If your skill level is equal o
 recipe, 100% of success rate.
- If your skill level is under o
 Success Rate = 100 - 9 *(minimu
 level).
 For example, the minimum skill 
 skill level is 7. The formula i
 rate.
 Under 11 levels the success rat

To raise the skill level, when
you success create/upgrade an
item with more low success rate,
more your experience bar will
increase. So I suggest you to
try to create/upgrade those
items since you don't gain too
much exp with 100% success rate
items and you don't lose the
materials when you failure in
its creation. But remember, it's
up to you and it's only my
opinion, so you can raise your
level more slowly with 100%
success rate recipes (or near
it).


********************************
5.1. Accessory [Accessory]
********************************

Show that you can be a fashion
villager by making gorgeous
accessories to use or just to
give as gifts to anyone you
like. Also, accessories can be
used as specials equipments to
boost your status or give new
abilities to your character.

In order to start crafting
accessories, talk to Yue on
Monday and buy the Forge /
Workshop Station. To get shelves
to store materials, wait until
Wednesday and buy it from Yue.

To learn new recipes you can go
to Mana's and Barrett's class at
school, they will teach how to
prepare different accessories.
Another way is, if you already
know the recipe (like reading a
walkthrough), you can start
creating new accessories
immediately, if you have the
necessary materials. Also you
can try to mix some random
materials (if use some logic on
it), maybe you can get a result.
A learned recipe will be
registered in your book at
Accessories Table's options.

To save time of collecting
materials (or just to save them
for better creations), you can
concentrate in upgrading
accessories, since it doesn't
consume too many materials. The
max level of upgrade is 10, but
you can still keep upgrading to
raise your skills.

The recipes are ordered by
creation/upgrade, by their type
and finally by the skill level.
They'll follow the model shown
just below:


Recipe
--------------------------------
Description: Original text from
game. Skill Level: The minimum
level required to make this
forgery with 100% success
Materials: What ingredients you
need. Learn From: From where you
learn this recipe. Selling
Price: How much you can sell.

********************************
5.2. Forging                    
********************************

If you want something well done,
do it by yourself. To get the
best weapons, improve their
status and also increase the
charge from your farm's tools,
this skill is absolutely
necessary in your gameplay.

In order to start forging, talk
to Yue on Monday and buy the
Forge / Workshop. To get shelves
to store materials, wait until
Wednesday and buy it from Yue.

To learn new recipes you can go
to Barrett's class at school, he
will teach how to prepare
different forges. Another way is
if you already know the recipe
(like reading a walkthrough).
Also you can try to mix some
random materials (if use some
logic on it), maybe you can get
a result. A learned recipe will
be registered in your book at
Forging Anvil's options.

To save time of collecting
materials (or just to save them
for better creations), you can
concentrate in upgrading weapons
since it doesn't consume too
much materials. The max level of
upgrade is 10, but you can still
keep upgrading to raise your
skills.

The recipes are ordered by
creation/upgrade, by their type
and finally by the skill level.
They'll follow the model shown
just below:

Recipe
--------------------------------
Description: Original text from
game. Skill Level: The minimum
level required to make this
forgery with 100% success
Materials: What ingredients you
need. Learn From: From where you
learn this recipe. Selling
Price: How much you can sell.

********************************
5.3. Pharmacy [Pharmacy]
********************************

In order to start creating
medicine, talk to Yue on Monday
and buy the Pharmacy Station. To
get a refrigerator to store food
and alike, wait until Wednesday
and buy it from Yue.

In order to start creating
medicine, talk to Yue on Monday
and buy the Pharmacy Station. To
get a refrigerator to store the
ingredients, wait until
Wednesday to buy it from Yue.

To learn new recipes you can go
to Mana's and Barrett's classes
at school, they will teach how
to prepare different medicines.
When you kill the dungeon's
guardians and check the statue
closing a room entrance,
different recipes will be taught
to you as a reward for
completing the task. Another way
is if you already know the
recipe (like reading a
walkthrough). Also you can try
to mix some random ingredients
(if use some logic on it), maybe
you can get a result. A learned
recipe will be registered in
your book at Pharmacy Table's
options.

To raise Pharmacy there isn't a
best way to do it, so try to
create complementary ingredients
for cooking (Sour Drop, Heavy
Spice and Sweet Powder for
example), items that can help
you in farming or to explore
dungeons (like Greenifiers,
Formulas, Potions for example),
recipes that you can buy
ingredients from shop (Antidote,
Roundoff, Para-gone, etc), just
choose what is the best to you
in the moment.

The level of the item created
will be equal to the mean of all
the levels of the ingredients
used to make this item. For
example, if you mix a Red Grass
(level 7) and a Red Grass (level
2), using a simple Mean Formula:
(7 + 2) / 2 = 4.5, so you will
create a Heavy Spice level 4
(result rounded down).

The recipes are ordered by the
skill level. They'll follow the
model shown just below:

Recipe
--------------------------------
Description: Original text from
game. Skill Level: The minimum
level required to make this dish
with 100% success Ingredients:
What ingredients you need. Learn
From: From where you learn this
recipe. Effect: What the item do
when used. Selling Price: How
much you can sell.


Recovery Potion
--------------------------------
Description: A pale green liquid
medicine. Drink for 100 HP
recovery. Skill Level: 6
Ingredients: Empty Bottle, Green
Grass, Medicinal Herb Learn
From: Medicinal Basics (Tuesday
Mana's Lessons) Effect: Recovery
100 HP Selling Price: -


Heavy Spice
--------------------------------
Description: Spice made from
spicy leaves. Eat it raw, and
you'll be spewing
    fire before you know it.
Skill Level: 10 Ingredients: Red
Grass, Red Grass Learn From:

********************************
5.4. Cooking                    
********************************

After taking a good care of your
animals and collect their stuff,
growing up the vegetables and
fruits on your farm, you can
make a good use of them. Prepare
the favorites dishes of a
villager as a gift and give to
him/her, show to everyone your
cooking skills or simple do a
more expensive item to sell.

In order to start forging, talk
to Yue on Monday and buy the
Large Kitchen (the small one
only allows to use the Pot,
Frying Pan and Knife, while the
large one offers all this and
the oven, steamer and mixer). To
get a refrigerator to store food
and alike, wait until Wednesday
and buy it from Yue. You can buy
the utensils on Friday.

To learn new recipes you can go
to Mana's class at school, she
will teach how to prepare
different dishes and what
utensils you need. Another way
is if you already know the
recipe (like reading a
walkthrough). Also you can try
to mix some random ingredients
(if use some logic on it), maybe
you can get a result. A learned
recipe will be registered in
your book at utensils options.

Different from other items
creation, when you failed to
cook your ingredients will be
lost, creating an item called
"Failed Dish", so be careful
with it (you use save/load to
avoid this). To raise Cooking
there isn't a best way to do it,
so try to create complementary
ingredients for cooking (Bread,
Butter, Rice Ball for example),
recipes that have easy materials
to get, recipes near the minimum
level required, just choose what
is the best to you in the
moment.

The level of the item will be
equal to the mean of all the
levels of the ingredients used
to make this item. For example,
if you fry a Rice (level 1), a
Carrot (level 3), a Curry Powder
(level 1), a Green Pepper (level
2), an Onion (level 3) and an
Oil (level 1), using a simple
Mean Formula: (1 + 3 + 1 + 2 + 3
+ 1) / 6 = 1.8333, so you will
create a Dry Curry level 1
(result rounded down).

The recipes are ordered by the
utensil needed and the skill
level. They'll follow the model
shown just below:

Recipe
--------------------------------
Description: Original text from
game. Skill Level: The minimum
level required to make this dish
with 100% success Ingredients:
What ingredients you need. Learn
From: From where you learn this
recipe. Effect: What the item do
when used. Selling Price: How
much you can sell.

********************************
5.5. Wi-Fi Evolution [Wifi]
********************************

In this game, besides leveling
up your weapons and accessories,
you can also evolve them by
trading specific high level
items with your friends via
Wireless or Nintendo Wi-Fi
Connection. To do so, all you
need to do is to have the
correct level 10 item with you
and start a wireless connection
by interacting with the mirror
in the bedroom of your house,
after that, find someone you
want to trade items with and
start trading. If you send (or
receive) a level 10 weapon or
accessory that can evolve, a
message will alert your friend
(or you) that the item has
changed. When that happens, a
new evolved and more powerful
item will be received on the
other side at level 1 (don't
worry, it's still more powerful
than before). Of course you can
also upgrade the new item up to
level 10 again and increase even
more its power.

Just in case you don't know, in
order to get higher level items,
follow the upgrade steps
described in the corresponding
section above.

The sections below explain which
item you need to trade and what
it'll evolve to once it reaches
the other player. The
accessories are ordered
alphabetically and the weapons
by attack power.


================================
5.5.1. Accessory Wi-Fi Evolution
       [Accessory-Wifi]
================================

--------------------------------
Description: A scroll detailing
the secrets of attacking. Evolve
from: Courage Badge Selling
Price: 2650G

--------------------------------
Description: A scroll detailing
the secrets of defense. Evolve
from: Talisman Selling Price:
1410G

--------------------------------
Description: A scroll detailing
the secrets of magic. Evolve
from: Magic Earring Selling
Price: 3590G

--------------------------------

awarded to those who have
obtained complete and total

################################
6. Fighting                     
################################

In Rune Factory series, fighting
is an important part of the
game, since you'll need to do
this a lot once you start
entering the dungeons available.
This section will present some
info concerning fighting, the
weapons and Rune Abilities of
the game.


********************************
6.1. Elemental Attributes
     [Attributes]
********************************

There are six Elemental
Attributes in this game and they
affect the damage taken /
inflicted when an elemental
equipment or monster faces
another elemental enemy.

There are three pairs of
opposing elemental:

- Fire and Water
- Wind and Earth
- Light and Darkness

The relationship of the
elementals in one pair is as
follows: the damage inflicted by
one of the elements on the other
one is increased so, if, for
example, a fire-type weapon hits
a water-type monster, the
damaged will be increased, since
they're opposing elementals. On
the other hand, if an elemental
attack of the same type as the
elemental defense is used, the
damage will be decreased, for
example, a wind-type attack
against a wind-type monster will
deal less damage than it should.


********************************
6.2. Status Ailments [Ailments]
********************************

Sometimes you'll be affected by
some Status Ailments during the
game, not only by fighting
monsters but also for not
sleeping well, stepping on
venom, etc.. If you're affected
by any status at the moment, a
status icon will appear just
below the HP and RP bar in the
upper left corner of the screen.
You can touch and hold it to see
the status name.

I'll list below the status that
can be inflicted upon you as you
play, what it does and how to
heal it.

All Status Ailments may be
healed, besides the way I tell
below in each of them, by asking
Natalie to heal you in the
clinic ("I'm not feeling very
well." option). She'll charge
you 100G.

- Cold: Triples the RP consumpti
 to bed late (after AM 3:00) and
 twice without healing). Can be 
 early doesn't work).
- Fatigue: Doubles the RP consum
 go to bed late (after AM 3:00) 
 understand). Can be healed by s
- Paralysis: You can't run while
 eating a Para-Gone.
- Poison: Takes damage constantl
 stop inflicting damage either a
 Can be healed by eating an Anti
- Seal: You can't activate Rune 
  healed by eating a Roundoff.

Also there is one beneficial
status, "Food", it'll appear
after you consume an item (Raw
crops, dishes, some medicines)
and will boost some specific
stats for a time. Each item
gives a different effect and
have different duration periods
(check the Pharmacy and Cooking
section to know those effects).


********************************
6.3. Accessories [Accessories]
********************************

Accessories provides a lot of
kinds of bonuses for the
character and you should have
some of them for each situation
you face. Bonuses may include
additional defense, attributes,
protection against elementals,
status ailments, etc.

* Second generation only.

********************************
6.4. Weapons                    
********************************

In order to fight properly and
be able to face the monster the
best way possible, it's
important to know the equipment
you can choose so that it'll fit
your style.

That said, I'll show a list of
the weapons I've seen so far and
its status so that it can help
you in your decision. Notice the
items are considered to be level
1.

* Second generation only


================================
6.4.1. Axe                      
================================

It has a nice attack power, only
lower than a hammer, and also
have a high critical rate ratio.
It works in a similar way as the
hammer, but do not knock out the
enemies. Choose this over the
hammer if you want to get more
critical hits. Even though this
is a great weapon to dealing a
lot of damage in one strike, its
attacks are very slow, making it
a bit difficult to fight with.
Notice that, by using the axe as
a weapon you won't increase the
Weapons skill level, but instead
the Logging one. You can also
chop wood with this weapon, the
same way as the farming axe.


Battle-Axe
--------------------------------
How to get: Buy from The Sharper
Edge Blacksmithing for 1200G.
Description: An axe with a wild,
uncontrolled swing. Handle with
care. Effect: - Attribute: -
Attack: 28 Charge: 1

================================
6.4.2. Hammer                   
================================

It has the highest attack power
of all weapons. Its powerful
strikes allows you to knock out
foes and keep them away from
you. Even tough you inflict a
large damage and keep enemies
away, you need to be careful
when facing more than one foe at
once or when you're fighting
against a quick enemy, since
this is a very slow weapon and
require some ability to use it
effectively. Notice that, by
using the hammer as a weapon
you'll increase the Mining skill
level, instead of the Weapons
one. You can also mine and break
rocks with this weapon, the same
way as the farming hammer.

--------------------------------
How to get: Buy from The Sharper

Effect: -

Charge: 1

================================
6.4.3. Longsword [Longsword]
================================

Stronger than shortswords,
allows you to hit enemies hard
and from a safer distance, since
this weapon has a longer reach.
This one also have a high
critical hit ratio and the swing
affects a large area, so you'll
be able to do a lot of damages
more times and strike more
enemies at once. On the other
hand, you can only chain few
attacks and the first strike is
slow.

================================
6.4.4. Rod                      
================================

It's not a good weapon by
itself, due to its very low
attack power. However, it's a
nice pick for a conjurer,
because most, if not all, of
them increases your intelligence
attribute and hence your magic
power, allowing you to cast more
powerful Rune Abilities.
Additionally, this is one of the
weapons, besides the shortsword,
that allows you to equip a
shield and improve your defense.
Even tough it's very versatile,
since there are a good variety
of Rune Abilities that can
benefit from this bonus, you
need to be careful about your
RP, because, unlike the other
weapons, the Rune Abilities
cannot be casted after you
deplete all your RP by consuming
HP, so you should always have
another weapon at your disposal
just in case you need it in the
middle of a fight, as I really
don't recommend trying to fight
using the rod itself, since it's
very weak and can't chain
attacks. Notice as well there
aren't Skill Seals for rods so
it's a bit more limited.


Rod
--------------------------------
How to get: Buy from The Sharper
Edge Blacksmithing for 1200G.
Description: A staff that boosts
magical power. Was not designed
to be used as
    a weapon itself.
Effect: Int up (Magic Attack
+21, Magic Def +5, Int + 12)
Attribute: - Attack: 3 Charge: 1

================================
6.4.5. Shortsword [Shortsword]
================================

Allows you to defeat your
enemies by unleashing a rapid
series of attacks. Even though
the attacks are quick they're
not so strong and be careful
about the last strike, since it
lets you very vulnerable. This
is one of the two weapons that
allows you to equip a shield at
the same time, the other being
the rod, improving your defense
and hence, decreasing the damage
taken. Nice pick for beginners,
but also good for some veterans.

================================
6.4.6. Spear                    
================================

Very high reach. With these
you'll be able to hit enemies
from afar and keep a safe
distance to avoid more damage.
It has a moderate attack power
and some of them increases your
defense when equipped. Even
though the attack has a long
reach, because it's a pierce
attack you'll need to take some
care when aiming at the enemy.
It's also kind of difficult to
deal with lots of enemies at
once, unless they're disposed in
a line formation.

********************************
6.5. Shields                    
********************************

Shields are only useful if
you're fighting with a
shortsword or a rod, since no
other weapon allows you to equip
a shield at the same time (the
shield bonus will not be applied
if you equip another weapon).
So, if you like to use the
shortsword or cast magics to
fight, you really should take
advantage of this defense bonus
that, as you unlock new shields,
may affect significantly the
damage you take from monsters
you fight against.

--------------------------------
How to get: Buy from The Sharper
Edge Blacksmithing for 500G.
Description: A small, easy-to-
use shield that offers only
limited defense. Effect: -
Attribute: - Defense: 2

********************************
6.6. Magic Books [Magics]
********************************

Magic Books are referred in this
guide as Rune Abilities, just as
the Skill Seals are. Don't think
they're the same, though. Magic
Books allows you to cast magic
spells on enemies to inflict
damage or in yourself to heal HP
/ Status. To improve the magic
effect you need to repair the
magic books by bringing them to
Mana at Alvarna Academy -
Classroom, but she can only fix
it if you bring the book and the
right Missing Page in order
(that means Mana can't restore a
more advanced page if you don't
have the previous ones). The
Missing Pages can be get as
quest's rewards. As for Skill
Seals, see the next section.

* Second generation only

********************************
6.7. Skill Seals [Seals]
********************************

Skill Seals are referred in this
guide as Rune Abilities, just as
the Magic Books are. Unlike the
Magic Books, the Skill Seals are
weapon dependent and can only be
casted if you're equipped with
the proper weapon for that seal.
Combo Attack types means that
skill do different moves if you
keep hitting the button.

* Second generation only.

the gap between enemies in a
    flash.

attack everything in this space
as the description
    says, after starts moving, i

6.8. Musical Scores [Musical]
********************************

Musical scores are referred in
this guide as Rune Abilities,
just as the Skill Seals and
Spells are. Don't think they're
the same, though. Musical Scores
allows you to control monsters
skill.

* Second generation only.

--------------------------------
How to get: Build a barn and
enter. Mana will come and give
this to you. Description: A
sprightly tune. Allied monsters
will flash yellow and perform
    their best move successful.
Effect: Read the description.

    Inn (1st floor), you need to
Description: A rousing tune.

and go on a rampage
    when they hear it.

################################
7. Village                      
################################

This is where you and all of the
people you interact with live.
So it's important to know it
well and take advantage of
everything it can offer you.
Here you can find out about the
houses, shops, villagers,
festivals and quests you'll see
during the game.


********************************

********************************

Well, I'm really not good at
ASCII drawing, but I think this
map will help the players to
know where to go when needed.

Each of the 10 squares
correspond to an area of the
village. In the top of each
square is the name of that area
(the one that is shown in the
game) and in the middle of them
are some important spots you
should know.

To get access to Palermo Shrine,
please take a look at the
corresponding section in this
guide under Dungeons.

********************************
7.4. School                     
********************************

An important institution for any
town, where children go to learn
a lot of new things to help in
their education and become the
future of nation. The Alvarna
Academy is under the guidance of
good teachers (Mana and
Barrett), they'll teach many
important things in second
generation that you couldn't do
in the first one. This is only
available at second generation
and marks the end of the first
game arc. Mana's classes are
from AM 09:00 until AM 11:15.
Barret's start at PM 12:00

Kyle couldn't complete all
school's facilities, so it's up
to his descendants to finish
this task and give the kids more
options of learning (oh, how
cool you are, the children are
now really happy to have extra
lessons). Check out the
Buildings/Expansions section to
get more details.

The Alvarna Academy is divided
in four different sections, you
can access them at anytime you
want, I'm going to list and
explain them all in the
following subsections.


================================
7.4.1. Classroom [Classroom]
================================

Mana and Barrett give important
lessons about cooking, forging,
medicine creation and other
stuffs. You can only have two
classes per day (I mean you can
only check two different topics
in the blackboard per day) with
each teacher, except on holidays
when you don't have class. Also
note that each day of the week
have different sets of topics.
After you have learned a lesson
it will disappear from the
options (except the first
lessons and, on Friday,
Barrett's first lesson will
disappear but Hammer Basics
won't).

Mana can be found in Alvarna
Academy - Classroom in the
morning (AM 09:00 - AM 11:05).
She'll teach you about cooking,
pharmacy and accessories
production, she can also repair
magic books, but only if you
bring the book and the right
Missing Page in order (that
means Mana can't restore a more
advanced page if you don't have
the previous ones). Next I'll
list her lessons topics and what
do you learn from them:

================================
7.4.2. Dojo                     
================================

After training your mind in
classroom and library, now you
need to train your body. You can
use the dojo just outside school
from AM 09:00 to PM 10:00. Just
enter, check the little board
inside and Barrett will come and
explain about the place if it's
your first time.

You can summon monsters in dojo
to fight against and they won't
be able to leave the place, so
it's a perfect place to raise
your skills in a safe way. If
you faint there, you'll be taken
to the clinic and the game won't
end as Barrett will supervise
your training. After completing
a challenge you'll be reward
with Skills Seals. To do the
next challenge you need to
complete first the previous ones
in order.


First Challenge
--------------------------------
Rewards: Triple Strike, Thrust
Strike and Hammer Fall Mission:
Defeat 5 monsters (in this
order):
- Orc
- Orc Archer
- Orc
- Orc Archer
- Orc


Second Challenge
--------------------------------
Rewards: Life Drain and Shine
Mission: Defeat 6 monsters (in
this order):
- Goblin Gangster
- Hammer Troll
- Hammer Troll
- Goblin Gangster
- Goblin Gangster
- Hammer Troll


Third Challenge
--------------------------------
Rewards: Dash Slash and Gale
Blade Mission: Defeat 7 monsters
(in this order):
- Shadow Panther
- Shadow Panther
- Shadow Panther
- Hornet
- Hornet
- Hornet
- Shadow Panther


Fourth Challenge
--------------------------------
Rewards: Flash Strike and Giant
Swing Mission: Defeat 8 monsters
(in this order):
- Little Wizard
- Aerian
- Little Wizard
- Aerian
- Aerian
- Little Wizard
- Aerian
- Little Wizard


Fifth Challenge
--------------------------------
Rewards: Rush Attack and Strong
Shot Mission: Defeat 9 monsters
(in this order):
- Claw Dragon
- Minotauros
- Minotauros
- Claw Dragon
- Minotauros
- Claw Dragon
- Claw Dragon
- Minotauros
- Claw Dragon


Sixth Challenge
--------------------------------
Rewards: Naive Blade and Hundred
Cracker Mission: Defeat 10
monsters (in this order):
- Orc
- Orc Archer
- Hammer Troll
- Goblin Gangster
- Shadow Panther
- Hornet
- Little Wizard
- Aerian
- Claw Dragon
- Minotauros


================================
7.4.3. Library                  
================================

The quiet place where you can
read a lot of interesting books.
This facility don't have too
much to offer, you can take the
Stone Spike and Sonic Wind spell
books (just after it has been
build), also you can play
Sugoroku with your friends.
Other skills and items can be
found in this place in the right
moment (they will be informed at
the right sections).


================================
7.4.4. Workshop [Workshop]
================================

This place is where you can do
the most different creations in
game, like cooking and forging.
All the equipments are available
to use as you want, but you need
to buy the stations first in
Yue's Bargains shop on Mondays
and the tools/utensils on
Wednesdays (check it on Shops
section).

Douglas will come here in
everyday from PM 12:00 to PM
01:59 and offer a free lunch to
the students, but the dish
varies from day to day.

Like your house, there is a lot
of things you can use, so I'll
try to give a brief explanation
about the item and utensil you
can interact with in the
workshop. You can interact with
them by getting close to one of
them and pressing the action
button or touching the screen.

I'll start from the one in the
upper left corner and proceed to
the right until the wall and
then I'll go back to the left
again and go down. So here's the
list:

Full Set of Tools: Allows you to
process your products. From left
to right -
    Mayonnaise Maker, Cheese Mak
Refrigerator: You can store food
and alike here. Shelf: You can
store non-eatable items you
don't use frequently here.
Steamer: Use to steam your
ingredients and prepare
delicious dishes. Mixer: Use to
make refreshing juices. Oven:
Use to roast or bake. Pot: Use
to cook delicious food. Frying
Pan: Use to fry. Knife Set: Use
to prepare some dishes like
sashimi. Empty Cooking Table:
Use to prepare dishes that don't
require anything else. Forging
Anvil: Use to forge and
strengthening weapons and
armors. Accessories Table: Use
to make gorgeous accessories.
Pharmacy Table: Use to create
medicines. Record Player: Use to
listen the theme season's songs
from your farm.


********************************
7.5. Buildings/Expansions
     [Buildings]
********************************

This section explains the
different buildings in the game
and what you need to make or
expand them. To order these
buildings and expansions, talk
to Byron (when he is at his
house) and invest your money to
create a better place to live
for your friends. For Workshop
expansions (stations) talk to
Yue and select "I want a
bargain." on Mondays (in others
days she sells different stuffs
or simply don't sell bargains).

The constructions will be
ordered as they appear in the
game and follow the model shown
just below:

--------------------------------

building/expansion. Requirement:

to do this building/expansion.

wood needed. Notes: Some
information about

********************************
7.6. Quests - First Generation
     [Quests1]
********************************

The header below is an example
of how the quests are disposed.
Each character's quest is in a
different section identified by
his/her name. Inside that
section you'll see one table for
each quest that character
requests you. The tables are
sorted by request order of that
character.

Each table contains: the title
of the quest, the description
you can see in the game, what
you need to fulfill before
taking that quest, the
friendship or love level in
which the character will request
that quest, what you can obtain
by completing it and at last, an
explanation of what you should
do to finish it.

Just a note, for some quest read
the section How to Complete
before you go to talk to the
person who gives the quest, so
you can take the asked item
first and save some time (only
recommended for such item like
monster's drops or commons
(grass, mining rocks,
fruits...)). For monsters
hunting quests, you can take a
tamed monster with you to help
and complete it more easily.

To start a new quest, go and
check the Bulletin Board at De
Sainte-coquille Park until 6 PM.
In festival days and after that
time you can't start a new quest
anymore, however if you already
have start a new one, you still
can complete it (in festivals
days too).

Notes:
- The next quest of a character 
 previous one from that same per
 appear to avoid blocking the ne
- After a girl get married, if y
 disappear from bulletin board. 
- "Gate" is the name of the sphe
 call it like this in the quests


================================
Character Name
================================

Quest Name
--------------------------------
Description: Original text from
game Requirement: What you need
to start the quest Love Level or
Friendship Level: Required
friendship level or love level
with
    requester to unlock this que
    example some character asks 
    actually get the level)
Reward: What you will earn after
completing the quest (all quests
will raise a
    little the friendship/love p

How to Complete: What you need
to do in order to finish the
quest

7.6.4. Cammy                    
================================

Super Training Plan: Strength!
--------------------------------
Description: Improve your
strength with shadow boxing!
Requirement: Have talked to
Cammy at least once before and
completed "Please
    Deliver Something for Me" (M
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: Toyherb Seed

How to Complete: Talk to Cammy.
She'll say if you go through her
training you'll become a Super-
Kyle (or the name you choose for
your character), wow! Seriously,
the game is not that difficult,
she'll say a sequence of four
punches (either left or right
each) and after that she'll ask
you to repeat them one at a time
at the same order she said.
There is no need to rush, just
pay attention to what she says,
take note if you think it'll be
necessary, and then just choose
the same directions she said.
This will be repeated four
times, and if you manage to do 3
out of the 4 correctly you'll
win and finish the quest. If you
couldn't, just talk to her again
and she'll restart the training.
By the way, you won't earn a
better reward if you do all the
sequences correctly, so don't
bother if you miss one of them.


Super Training Plan: Luck!
--------------------------------
Description: Improve your luck
with rock paper scissors!
Requirement: Have completed
Cammy's first quest: "Super
Training Plan:
    Strength!"
Friendship Level: Between 1 and
2 Reward: Tomato Seed

How to Complete: Talk to Cammy.
Your personal trainer prepared
the second part of your train to
become the Super-Kyle. And for
that it is essential to raise an
important attribute for any
superhero, your luck in Rock,
Paper, Scissors (RPS), since
this is a very dangerous battle
until death. Cammy won't take
easy and your battle consist in
10 matches and you need to
choose one command (rock, paper
or scissors) and win at least 6
of the matches (see below a
winning strategy). If you win,
you'll be one step closer from
your final form and a lot more
prepared to defeat any villain
with your RPS combat style.

Winning Strategy in RPS
(contributed by a.tran): Cammy's
choices actually follow a
pattern. And it is possible to
predict what she is going to
choose next.

The first round of RPS is pure
luck. However starting on the
second round you can begin
manipulating the game.

I will show you a few rounds of
RPS as an example, then explain
the pattern (Keep in mind the
first round is pure luck)

R1: Me: Rock (Random choice) R1:
Cammy: paper (Her random answer)
R2: Me: Scissors (Winning
choice) R2: Cammy: Paper (Her
pattern choice) R3: Me: Paper
(Winning choice) R3: Cammy: Rock
(Her pattern choice) R4: Me:
Rock (...) R4: Cammy: Scissors

This is kind of difficult to
explain, but once you catch on
it will all make sense.

For example, if you picked Rock
on the first round (a random
choice), you'll have no idea
what Cammy will choose in this
round. But you'll know what
she'll choose in the next one.
Alright, so you pick rock, and
say she picks paper. Cammy wins
Round one.

In the next round, Cammy will
choose paper because it beats
rock which is what you picked in
the previous round. Because you
know she'll choose paper, you'll
choose scissors (a winning
choice) so you can beat her. By
the same logic, you also know
that Cammy will choose rock on
the next round, because rock
beats scissors which is what you
chose in this round. Since you
know that Cammy will pick rock,
you must choose paper to beat
her.

In short: Cammy will choose
whichever element
(rock/paper/scissors) that is
superior to the element you
picked in the previous round.
Since you know that, you will
choose whichever element is
superior to her in the current
round because she is choosing
whichever is superior to you in
the last round.

This logic may be a bit
difficult to understand, so if
you didn't get it by the
explanation above, don't worry,
just proceed according to the
instructions below:

- First Round: Choose any elemen
- Starting from the second round
    - If you chose Rock in the p
    - If you chose Paper in the 
    - If you chose Scissors in t

Following the instructions above
you should be able to win at
least 9 of the 10 round and thus
win the challenge.


Super Training Plan: Memory!
--------------------------------
Description: Improve your memory
with a quiz game! Requirement:
Have completed Cammy's second
quest: "Super Training Plan:
Luck!" Friendship Level: Between
2 and 3 Reward: Pineapple Seed

How to Complete: Talk to Cammy.
A new chapter on an hero's
training begins now. In this
session you'll improve your
brainpower with Memory Games,
remember, with a good memory you
can save your life in such
crucial moments like when you
are on bathroom and the paper
ends, if you had remember before
that happens, you won't get in
this dangerous situation. Ok,
back to the game, Cammy will say
some names and you need to
memorize them in order. If you
get one answer wrong it will
start all over again.
- Round One: Cammy says "Banana,
name of the third fruit
(Orange).
- Round Two: Cammy says "Pepper,
the name of the first vegetable
(Pepper).
- Round Three: Cammy says "Tuna,
second fish (Salmon). After
answering all correct Cammy will
congratulate you for a such good
memory and give your reward.


Super Training Plan: Etiquette!
--------------------------------
Description: Improve your
etiquette by learning table
manners! Requirement: Have
completed Cammy's third quest:
"Super Training Plan:
    Memory!"
Friendship Level: Between 3 and

How to Complete: Heroes never
stop! Talk to Cammy, it's time

festival in your tribute and to
not be rude in your own party.
She'll ask some questions and
you need to answer 4 of them
right. The questions are
following:

- Question 1: "What is the prope
Answer: "Fold it in half and put
it on your lap."

- Question 2: "What is the prope
Answer: "Eat it a little at a
time, with a spoon."

- Question 3: "What is the prope
Answer: "Knife in right hand,
fork in left."

- Question 4: "What is the prope
Answer: "Break it up into bite-
sized pieces."

- Question 5: "What is the first
Answer: "Shine a light on it to
check the color."

After that "difficult" questions
(I don't know why I listed since
it's a little stupid to know
what to answer, but whatever)
and take your prize.

you answer "Will you marry me?"

Cecilia (a good prize!) and your
wedding will start automatically
after that. If choose any option
to finish this quest except get
married with Cecilia, the quest
will be canceled but you can
still start it over again
whatever you want (it will stay
on bulletin board until Cecilia
or you get married).

7.6.8. Egan

Please Taste This for Me
--------------------------------
Description: I've made something

    is fine with me, so please s
Requirement: Have talked to Egan

Friendship Level: 0
Reward: Clippers

How to Complete: Talk to Egan.
He'll tell he's trying to think
up some new recipes for the
customers and he wants someone
to try them out. He'll then give
a new fish dish he made and will
ask your opinion about it. I'm
not sure if this changes
anything, such as friendship,
but if you answer "Try making it
really spicy.", he'll say your
response is not very reasonable.
The same applies to the "Try
adding a lot of vinegar.".
Choosing these options slightly
change the final dialogue, but
you'll get the reward the same
way, no matter your answers.

So, if you want to be sure and
give the best answers, choose
"Try adding more salt." and "Try
adding a little wine.", this way
Egan will tell you really helped
to make something better for the
customers.

Going to the Forest?
--------------------------------
Description: I have something to
take care of in forest. If
anyone is headed
    there, I would like to talk 
Requirement: Have completed
Egan's second quest: "I'm
Running Out of
    Ingredients"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: 500G

How to Complete: Talk to Egan.
He needs an Apple to give it to
Cecilia. Go to Trieste Forest
- Grassy Path. When you arrive i
from the apple tree just above
the Gate which spawn Orcs.
Notice this is the same tree
that produces apples regularly
each 3 days, and a new apple
won't be produced specifically
for this quest so, if you
already gathered them one or two
days ago, you won't find the
apples in the tree until you
wait the three days regrow time.
But, if the tree doesn't have
any apple and you don't want to
wait some days, there is still a
way. All you need to do is to go
the second area in this same
dungeon: Trieste Forest - Spring
Clearing and defeat some Pomme
Pomme (the red ball shaped
monster) in this area, as they
drop apples when defeated.
Remember the monster only spawns
during day, so if it's night
there's nothing you can do other
than waiting at least one day.
Finally, after getting the
apple, return it to Egan and get
your prize.

7.6.9. Gordon                   
================================

Please Get Me an Amethyst
--------------------------------
Description: I need you to get
this and bring it to me.
Requirement: Have talked to
Gordon at least once before and
completed "Please
    Deliver Something for Me" (M
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 400G

How to Complete: Talk to Gordon.
He'll tell you he wants you to
bring an Amethyst that can be
found in Blessia Island and
he'll give you a hammer. This
time the item won't be just
lying on the ground, you'll need
to use the hammer you got to
break the rocks in the island
and mine the amethyst from them.
Well, go to the port and take
the boat to Blessia Island. Once
there, explore the island
looking for the mining stones,
if you find some, break them
with your hammer and, if you
find a purple stone (Amethyst)
when you do this, you'll have
found the item you seek so go
back to the village and give it
to Gordon to receive the reward.

Just to let you know, there are
two stones you can break in
Blessia Island - South Beach
(after save point) and 7 stones
in Blessia Island - Center. If
you broke them all and, for some
reason, were unlucky and
couldn't find the Amethyst,
you'll have to wait until the
next day in order to be able to
mine from these stones once
again.


Please Get Me an Aquamarine
--------------------------------
Description: Sorry, but can you
get this for me too?
Requirement: Have completed
Gordon's first quest: "Please
Get Me an Amethyst" Friendship
Level: 1 Reward: 600G and 100
pieces of wood

How to complete: Talk to Gordon.
Like the previous quest he'll
ask you to get an ore, but this
time he'll request an Aquamarine
that can be found in Trieste
Forest. Break mining stones with
your hammer and, if you find a
blue stone (Aquamarine) go back
and give it to Gordon and
receive your reward. If you
already have an Aquamarine in
your possession, you can give it
to Gordon at once.

Just to let you know, there are
four stones you can break in
Trieste Forest - Aegis Falls. If
you broke them all and, for some
reason, were unlucky and
couldn't find the Aquamarine,
you'll have to wait until the
next day in order to be able to
mine from these stones once
again.


Please Get Me Some Sturdy String
--------------------------------
Description: As usual, I need
you to run and get something for
me. Requirement: Have completed
Gordon's second quest: "Please
Get Me an
    Aquamarine"
Friendship Level: 2
Reward: 600G

How to complete: Talk to Gordon.
For now he need a Strong String
(dropped by Spider), and as a
priest he can't go and fight
with those poor creatures. So
wait until night and go to
Trieste Forest - Grassy Path (2
Gates) or Trieste Forest -
Wooded Paradise (1 Gate spawning
both 1 ant and 1 spider). I
suggest you go to the first
option and keep killing until it
drops the item, but if you're
getting in trouble against 2
monsters at the same time,
destroy one Gate to make things
easier. Go back to Gordon and
finish the quest. If you already
have a Strong String in your
possession, you can give it to
Gordon at once.


Find a Diamond for Me
--------------------------------
Description: I want you to go
find a diamond for me. Come see
me for the
    details.
Requirement: Have completed
Gordon's third quest: "Please
Get Me Some Sturdy
    String"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: 700G

How to complete: Talk to Gordon.
Looks like he really collects
ores, so now you have to find a
Diamond to him, but it can be a
little difficult since it's a
rare item. Go to Padova
Mountains and break mining
stones with your hammer and, if
you find a Diamond go back and
give it to Gordon and receive
your reward.

Just to let you know, there are
eight stones that you can break
in Padova Mountains - Flowing
River and six more in Padova
Mountains - Freezing Cave. If
you broke them all and, for some
reason, were unlucky and
couldn't find the Diamond,
you'll have to wait until the
next day in order to be able to
mine from these stones once
again. If you already have a
Diamond in your possession, you
can give it to Gordon at once.

    for me!

--------------------------------
Description: There's something I

wanted to fight against him).

time but it's still a quest.

7.6.16. Ray                     
================================

Please Find Some Medicinal Herbs
--------------------------------
Description: Please find me some
medicinal herbs. Requirement:
Have talked to Ray at least once
before and completed "Please
    Deliver Something for Me" (M
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 50G

How to Complete: Talk to Ray and
he'll tell you he wants a
Medicinal Herb. As he says, this
herb grow everywhere, even on
the field on your farm. So just
go there and take it (it's one
of the green plants). If, for
some reason, you already cleaned
all your farm and don't have any
herbs with you, don't panic.
There's a lot of other ways to
get a Medicinal Herb. First of
all, you can go to any of the
four dungeons and take it from
the farming soil. Another way is
to just wait a day and look in
your farm again, since they can
grow everyday on untilled soil.
A last option is to buy from
Natalie (Alvarna Clinic) for
30G.

It doesn't matter how you get
it, after you do it, give the
herb to Ray and receive the
money.

--------------------------------
Description: I want you to help
my mom and my sister make up.
Requirement: Have completed

    Herbs"
Friendship Level: Between 1 and
2 Reward: A Thank You

How to Complete: Talk to Ray.
Natalie and Alicia are having an

and deliver it to Natalie,
restoring the peace in the
house. Report the events to Ray
and get your great prize
(discovering why Alicia and
Natalie complain about him).


Help Needed for On-Site Training
--------------------------------
Description: I want to do some
on-site training so I'm looking

    help me.

Ray's second quest: "Help Them
Make Up" Friendship Level:

(Ray will explain about the
day/night monsters). Ray will
take a look at you after the

completely your HP and RP and
give your prize.

7.6.17. Rosalind [Rosalind-Q1]

Please Find Me Some Lamp Grass
--------------------------------
Description: Could you please
supply me with some Lamp Grass?
(See me for
    details)
Requirement: Have talked to
Rosalind at least once before
and completed "Please
    Deliver Something for Me" (M
Love Level: 0
Reward: 2000G

How to Complete: Talk to
Rosalind and she'll give you
some direction on how to find
the Lamp Grass in Trieste
Forest. You won't be able to
actually see and pick this grass
as you could do with some other
items, Instead, you'll have to
follow her directions and, once
you walk through the right place
on the forest you'll
automatically notice the flower
growing at your feet and you'll
be asked whether you want to to
take it or not (obviously take
it when you find it).

Ok, so here's how you can find
the Lamp Grass. Enter Trieste
Forest and go to Trieste Forest
- Spring Clearing. Once you
enter this area, just keep
walking over the grass on the
right side, near the wooden
fence and you'll quickly be be
asked to take the grass. After
taking it, go back to Rosalind
and give her the item to claim
your valuable prize!


Please Find Me an Apple
--------------------------------
Description: I need a special
kind of apple from a specific
place. Could you
    please go and pick one for m
Requirement: Have completed
Rosalind's first quest: "Please
Find Me Some Lamp
    Grass"
Love Level: 1
Reward: 4000G and Harvest Basket

How to Complete: Talk to
Rosalind. She'll ask you to get
an Apple from Trieste Forest
since this place is too
dangerous for a lady. So as a
true gentleman go to Trieste
Forest
- Grassy Path. When you arrive i
from the apple tree just above
the Gate which spawn Orcs.
Notice this is the same tree
that produces apples regularly
each 3 days, and a new apple
won't be produced specifically
for this quest so, if you
already gathered them one or two
days ago, you won't find the
apples in the tree until you
wait the three days regrow time.
But, if the tree doesn't have
any apple and you don't want to
wait some days, there is still a
way. All you need to do is to go
the second area in this same
dungeon: Trieste Forest - Spring
Clearing and defeat some Pomme
Pomme (the red ball shaped
monster) in this area, as they
drop apples when defeated. I
know Rosalind asked specifically
the apples from the tree, but
she'll accept these apples as
well, so don't worry. Remember
the monster only spawns during
day, so if it's night there's
nothing you can't other than
wait at least one day. Finally,
after getting the apple, return
to Rosalind and get your prize.
