7.6.18. Roy                     
================================

I Need a Favor. Come Over?
--------------------------------
Description: Come talk to me...
I really messed something up...
Requirement: Have talked to Roy
at least once before and
completed "Please
    Deliver Something for Me" (M
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: Steamed Bread

How to Complete: Talk to Roy.
He'll ask you to bring him a
Cheap Cloth that can be obtained
by killing the orcs in Trieste
Forest. You'll want to have a
sword or some other weapon
before trying this quest. You
can also fight with your farming
tools, such as the hammer,
sickle, axe or even the hoe, but
the fight will be easier if you
have a real weapon, so it's your
choice. If you don't have one
but want to buy it, just take a
look at Tanya's shop (The
Sharper Edge Blacksmithing) and
you'll find them (the cheapest
is the spear, 1000G). If you
have the money pick the one you
think is the best for you.

Proceed to Trieste Forest.
You'll need to kill some club
orcs to find the Cheap Cloth.
They can be found on Trieste
Forest - Grassy Path or Trieste
Forest - Wooded Paradise during
day, that is, before PM 6:00. In
the Grassy Path, there are two
Gates that spawn the orc, so if
you think it's difficult to
fight against two of them at the
same time, try to destroy one of
the Gates, so that only one will
keep respawning orcs. In Wooded
Paradise, both monsters are
spawned by the same Gate, so
you'll have to deal with both at
the same time, just notice that
one of them is an Archer Orc and
it doesn't drop the item you
want when it's defeated.

After killing just a few orcs
you should be able to have one
of them to drop a chest. Open
the chest and you'll get the
Cheap Cloth. Go back to the
village and give it to Roy to
finish the job.


I Need Something Else
--------------------------------
Description: Something else
happened... Stop by for a
little? Requirement: Have
completed Roy's first quest: "I
Need a Favor. Come Over?"
Friendship Level: 1 Reward:
Pudding

How to complete: Talk to Roy.
More mess, now Roy broke a
Shoulder Piece (dropped by Orc
Viking) and you need to get
another one before his mother
notices. Go to Padova Mountains
- Crossroad or Padova Mountains
- Freezing Cave and kill the Orc
Viking until he drops the item
and then go back and deliver it
to Max and save another day. If
you already have the Shoulder
Piece with you, give it to Roy
at once.


I Could Use Your Help
--------------------------------
Description: I want to make
something and I could use your
help! Come see me! Requirement:
Have completed Roy's second
quest: "I Need Something Else"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: Charm

How to complete: Talk to Roy. He
didn't break anything now, in
truth he just want to know if
you have some kind of good-luck
charm to carry around. As you
don't have one, Roy'll ask you
to look for an Emerald to make
one to you (it looks like you're
popular with children). As
always, Emeralds can be found in
Trieste Forest. Break mining
stones with your hammer and, if
you find a green stone go back
and give it to Roy and receive
your reward. If you already have
an Emerald with you, give it to
Roy at once.

Again, just to let you know,
there are four stones you can
break in Trieste Forest - Aegis
Falls. If you broke them all
and, for some reason, were
unlucky and couldn't find the
Emerald, you'll have to wait
until the next day in order to
be able to mine from these
stones once again.


There's Something I Really Want
--------------------------------
Description: I want a ruby no
matter what happens. Come talk
to me. Requirement: Have
completed Roy's third quest: "I
Could Use Your Help" Friendship
Level: Near 3 Reward: Yam Seed

How to complete: Talk to Roy. He
needs a Ruby (since Cammy's got
one he doesn't have peace). So
Proceed to Blessia Island. Once
there, explore the island
looking for the mining stones,
if you find some, break them
with your hammer and, if you
find a red stone (Ruby) when you
do this, you'll have found the
item you seek so go back to the
village and give it to Roy to
receive the reward. If you
already have a Ruby with you,
give it to Roy at once.

Just to let you know, there are
two stones you can break in
Blessia Island - South Beach
(after save point) and 7 stones
in Blessia Island - Center. If
you broke them all and, for some
reason, were unlucky and
couldn't find the Ruby, you'll
have to wait until the next day
in order to be able to mine from
these stones once again. (and
yes, I'm using cut + paste)

Battle Strategies: Orc
--------------------------------
Description: There's something

Requirement: Have talked to
Tanya at least once before and
completed "Please
    Deliver Something for Me" (M
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 500G and Axe

How to Complete: Talk to Tanya.
Rather than a request, she'll
give you a trial. She wants you
to go to Trieste Forest and kill
5 orcs. You'll want to have a
sword or some other weapon
before trying this quest. You
can also fight with your farming
tools, such as the hammer,
sickle, axe or even the hoe, but
the fight will be easier if you
have a real weapon, so it's your
choice. If you don't have one
but want to buy it, just take a
look at Tanya's own shop and
you'll find them (the cheapest
is the spear, 1000G). If you
have the money pick the one you
think is the best for you.

Proceed to Trieste Forest.
You'll need to kill some club
orcs, archer orcs does not
count. They can be found on
Trieste Forest - Grassy Path or
Trieste Forest
- Wooded Paradise during day, th
are two Gates that spawn the
Orc, so if you think it's
difficult to fight against two
of them at the same time, try to
destroy one of the Gates, so
that only one will keep
respawning orcs. In Wooded
Paradise, both monsters are
spawned by the same Gate, so
you'll have to deal with both at
the same time, just notice that
one of them is an Archer Orc and
it doesn't count when it's
defeated.

If you defeat the correct
monster, you'll be alerted that
the one you killed is indeed the
target monster. So if you find
the one, defeat 5 of them
(you'll be notified again when
you reach your quota) and go
talk to Tanya again to claim
your reward. You can take this
quest again in the bulletin
board if you need money.

orcs does not count. They can be
found on Trieste Forest - Aegis
Falls or Trieste Forest
- Wooded Paradise. In Aegis Fall
Archer, but they're very far
from one another so I don't
think it'll change anything.
Anyway, if for some reason both
of the orcs come to fight
against you and you think it's
difficult to fight against both
of them at the same time, try to
destroy one of the Gates, so
that only one will keep
respawning the Orc Archer. In
Wooded Paradise, both monsters
are spawned by the same Gate, so
you'll have to deal with both at
the same time, just notice that
one of them is a club orc and it
doesn't count when it's
defeated.

If you defeat the correct
monster, you'll be alerted that
the one you killed is indeed the
target monster. So if you find
the one, defeat 8 of them
(you'll be notified again when
you defeat 5 of them and when
you reach your quota) and go

--------------------------------
Description: This time you'll be
tackling a Goblin Pirate! Quest
Can Be
    Replayed
Requirement: Have completed
Tanya's second quest: "Battle
Strategies: Orc
    (Continued)"
Friendship Level: 2
Reward: 1000G

How to Complete: Talk to Tanya.
As all Tanya's previous trials
you can repeat this one and you
need to kill 10 Goblin Pirates
(Goblin Gangster does not count)
for now, so you have 3 options
to go, Blessia Island - South
Beach (1 Gate), Blessia Island -
Altar/Old Ship (1 Gate) or
Blessia Island - Old Ship Deck
(1 Gate spawning both 1 Goblin
Gangster and 1 Goblin Pirate).
Choose the map which is most
suitable to you.

If you defeat the correct
monster, you'll be alerted that
the one you killed is indeed the
target monster. So if you find
the one, defeat 10 of them
(you'll be notified again when
you defeat 5 of them and when
you reach your quota) and go
talk to Tanya again to receive
the prize. You can take this
quest again in the bulletin
board if you need money.

Yue's Question (1)Match Answer
(2)Funny Answer (3)Normal Answer

Yue: What kind of food do you

(2)"Strange foods." (3)"Richer
foods."

Yue: What kind of music do you
like? (1)"Fast music."
(2)"Chanting monks." (3)"Slow
music."

Yue: What kind of clothes do you
like? (1)"Stylish clothing."
(2)"Comfortable clothing."
(3)"Underwear."

Yue: What kind of books do you
like? (1)"Dramatic Books."
(2)"Children's Books."
(3)"Adventure Novels."

Yue: Tell me something you don't
like. (1)"Selfish people."
(2)"Vegetables." (3)"Hurting
others."

After all this question gets
your reward.

7.7. Quests - Second Generation
     [Quests2]

The same as the previous
section, so same rules and
notes, but this time I'll list
the quests that appear in the
second generation part. Some
quests will only be available
for Aria and others only for

================================
7.7.1. Alicia's Quests
       [Alicia-Q2]
================================

Answer a Question for Me?
--------------------------------
Description: I want you to
answer me from your heart.
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level:
Between 2 and 3 Reward: Missing
Page 1 (Fireball)

How to Complete: Talk to Alicia.
If she is your mother, she will
ask you if she is a good mother.
If you answer "You're a good
mother.", Alicia will feel
better. If you answer "I'm not
sure." she'll say that she needs
to try a little harder and
finally if you answer "Not
really..." Alicia will get mad
(the funniest reaction).
Anyways, if you choose the first
or second option you'll receive
the reward, choosing the last
one only finishes the
conversation but you can talk to
her again and complete it. If
she isn't your mother, Alicia
will ask why do you think she
hasn't been able to find a man
yet. If you answer "Your love
reading didn't come true." or
"There's a problem with your
personality.", she will get mad
and you will need redo the
quest. If you answer "You're
just too beautiful!" she will be
happy and give a reward for your
"sincere" answer.

7.7.2. Barrett's Quests
       [Barrett-Q2]
================================

I Need Supplies for Class
--------------------------------
Description: I need you to get
me some materials to use in
class. Come see me
    for the details.
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level: 0
Reward: Missing Page 1 (Cure)

How to Complete: Talk to your
teacher (Barrett, in the case
you don't get the idea). He'll
ask you to get a Scrap Iron for
his next class. Do this favor
and get one for him. You can
find this item breaking the
mining stones from any dungeon,
it's the most common item to
get. Pick it up and give to him.
To thank you Barrett will give
you a reward for your efforts.


Something to Give to Jake
--------------------------------
Description: I have something
for Jake. Come talk to me for
more details. Requirement: Have
completed Barrett's first (2nd
generation) quest: "I Need
    Supplies for Class"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: Missing Page 1 (Water
Laser)

How to complete: Talk to
Barrett. He needs you to deliver
a Hard Horn to Jake for him, but
he doesn't know why Jake wants
it. Just do this extra exercise
(maybe you'll get more points in
your next test, it's always good
to help your teacher), meet Jake
and give it him, so he can do
his experiences. Go back and
tell the news to your teacher,
taking your reward. Note: If
you're reading this quest in
sequence, please read the next
one to collect the materials and
be prepared for when it appear.


About Class these Days
--------------------------------
Description: I have to talk to
you about class. Come here when
you can. Requirement: Have
completed Barrett's second (2nd
generation) quest: "Something
    to Give to Jake"
Friendship Level: Between 4 and
5 Reward: Smash Blade

How to complete: Talk to
Barrett. He finally notices that
some kids get bored during
classes (Roy in the case), so he
decides to give a pop quiz to
test his students (this always
happens because of someone in
class and everybody needs to
pay...). So Barrett wants you to
create Power Gloves for him to
test your knowledges. To
complete this quest you need
first to have expanded your
school, building a workshop and
bought the forge station from
Yue on Mondays. To make the item
(you can learn this lesson on
Thursday, at Advanced
Accessories topic), you need to
collect the following items:
Insect Skin (dropped by Ant),
Panther Claw (dropped by Shadow
Panther or Blood Panther),
Quality Cloth (dropped by Goblin
Pirate or Goblin Captain),
Strong String (dropped by
Spider), Giant's Gloves (dropped
by Hammer Troll) and Strong Vine
(use Inquisitive Waltz in
Blessia Island) and forging
level 19 (for success rate
100%), check the Forging Section
for further details. After you
complete it, talk to Barrett and
pass in your test.

Delivery for Dorothy
--------------------------------
Description: I need you to give

second generation Friendship
Level: 0 Reward: 600G

How to Complete: Talk to Byron.
Because of your kind nature (not
that kind as you always receive
something in the end), more
favors come. This time he will
ask you to deliver a Noel Grass
to Dorothy since she's running
low on medical supplies. Go
there and save her stock. Return
and complete the quest.


================================
7.7.4. Cammy's Quests [Cammy-Q2]
================================

Let's Have a Contest!
--------------------------------
Description: Let's have a
contest to see who can collect
more things! Requirement: Start
second generation Friendship
Level: 0 Reward: Ice Cream
(Winner prize) or Toyherb
(Consolation prize)

How to Complete: Talk to Cammy.
She is obsessed with collecting
Red Grass, but as it isn't funny
to play alone, she wants to
compete with you to see who can
get more of these. Since you're
probably doing this quest at the
first day of second generation,
there are a lot of them in your
farm, but you can also get them
from farming fields in dungeons
or simply buy them from Ray for
30G each. To win you need to get
six red grasses or more.


Give Something to Someone for Me
--------------------------------
Description: I'm too embarrassed
to give this to her myself. Can
you do it for
    me?
Requirement: Have completed
Cammy's first (2nd generation)
quest: "Let's Have a
    Contest!"
Friendship Level: 2
Reward: Heart Pendant

How to Complete: Talk to Cammy.
She made a present for her
sister (ooo, nice girl), but she
is too embarrassed to give it to
her, so she wants you to deliver
it to Dorothy. Meet her, give
the Heart Pendant and also tell
about Cammy and her intentions.
Go back and tell the news to
her, receiving the same gift
too.


I Have a Secret Plan
--------------------------------
Description: I thought of a
secret plan and I'm looking for
someone to help me
    me carry it out!
Requirement: Have completed
Cammy's second (2nd generation)
quest: "Give
    Something to Someone for Me"
Friendship and Love Level: 4
Reward: a participation on a
failed plan

How to complete: Talk to Cammy.
She will be at Alvarna Academy -
Classroom and she will explain
her secret plan: she wants to
sneak into school tonight. Cammy
will convince you to go with
her, so meet her at Alvarna
Academy at PM 09:00. Start a
conversation and follow her (she
made a secret passage, but the
doors are always unlocked, so I
don't know why she did it),
exploring the school during
night. After a while Barrett
will come and stop your playing.
In the end Cammy and you will
move out of the school and go
home.


I Want to Go Somewhere
--------------------------------
Description: There's somewhere I
want to go see. How about we go
together? Requirement: Have
completed Cammy's third (2nd
generation) quest: "I Have a
    Secret Plan" and be playing 
Friendship and Love Level: 6
Reward: A kiss on the cheek

How to complete: Talk to Cammy.
She have heard about an enormous
tree in Trieste Forest and want
to see it for herself. Since no
grownup will accept this idea,
Cammy decided to ask your help
because she knows that you've
already fought some monsters.
After some talk she will
convince you to go, so meet her
at Trieste Forest Entrance.
Cammy will just rush inside the
forest, so keep following her
(she'll go to Trieste Forest -
Spring Clearing, Aegis Fall,
River Stream, Sun-Dappled Spot
and finally to Great Tree).
After seeing it, Cammy will show
some snack that she brought for
a picnic and you both will eat a
Cookie. In the end Cammy wants
to thank you and give a present
but you just ate it, so she will
give another thing.


Come and See Me!
--------------------------------
Description: Come over! I have
something for you to do. I'll be
waiting! Requirement: Have
completed Cammy's fourth (2nd
generation) quest: "I Want to
    Go Somewhere" and be playing
Friendship and Love Level: 8
Reward: Cammy as girlfriend?

How to complete: Talk to Cammy.
She will finally confess that
she have liked you for a while
and will also ask how do you
fell about her. If you answer "I
like you a lot, Cammy...",
She'll be really happy and will
say that you are SO in love.
After some more talk, Cammy will
ask to her dad to help with
yours wedding (also you will see
some funny reactions from
Gordon) and two days will pass.
But if you answer "You're great
to hang out with!" the quest
will be abandoned, but you can
start again.


================================
7.7.5. Cecilia's Quests
       [Cecilia-Q2]
================================

Let's Cook Together!
--------------------------------
Description: Let's make some
candy together! Meet me at the
school? Requirement: Have an
oven (and all other requisites
for it) Friendship Level:
Between 2 and 3 Reward: Missing
Page 2 (Fireball)

How to Complete: Talk to
Cecilia. She will ask if you
want to make a Chocolate Cake
and meet her at school (Alvarna
Academy - Workshop). Go there
and start another conversation.
Now she will ask about what
ingredients you need to bake a
Chocolate Cake. If you answer it
wrong, Cecilia will get a little
angry and will ask if you want
to try again. If you answer
"Maybe later..." the quest will
be abandoned (when you accept
the quest again Cecilia will be
at school). To answer all
correct, choose "Butter",
"Milk", "Wheat Flour" and
"Chocolate". After this Cecilia
will start to sing and bake the
cake (cute, don't you think?).
When she is done, you both will
eat the Chocolate Cake and Cecil
will thank you for this day and
give a little gift to you.

7.7.10. Herman's Quests
        [Herman-Q2]
================================

A Quest for Dinner
--------------------------------
Description: There's something I
absolutely must have for dinner!
Please get it
    for me!
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level:
Between 0 and 1 Reward: 15000G

How to Complete: Talk to Herman.
Now for dinner time another
essential dish in any proper De
Sainte-coquille family dinner is
missing. He wants you to bring a
Fried Lover Snapper. To do this
check the cooking section to
know how to make this dish, but
notice you will need to have
cooking level near 71 and a
kitchen with a frying pan. Lover
Snappers can be found at Trieste
Forest - Sun-Dapplet Spot (check
the map to locate the hidden
river) or in Alvarna Pond during
Spring. After cooking, go back
and deliver it to Herman.


A Quest for a Snack
--------------------------------
Description: There is a snack
that I absolutely must have!
Please get it for
    me!
Requirement: Have completed
Herman's first (2nd generation)
quest: "A Quest for
    Dinner"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: 30000G

How to Complete: Talk to Herman.
Now for tea time another
essential dish in any proper De
Sainte-coquille family dinner is
missing. He wants you to bring a
Cheesecake. To do this check the
cooking section to know how make
this dish, but you will need to
have cooking level near 41 and a
kitchen with oven (if you have
cooked the dish from previous
quest this isn't a problem for
now). To bake one you need
Cheese, Cookie, Egg and Flour
(all these items can be bought
in Pumpkin General Store and you
need to have the Full Set of
Tools from Yue to transform Milk
into Cheese). After cooking, go
back and deliver it to Herman.

7.7.11. Jake's Quests [Jake-Q2]
================================

Get Me Swordmaking Materials
--------------------------------
Description: I don't have enough
materials to make swords. If you
get some for me, I'll give ya
something good. Requirement:
Start second generation
Friendship Level: Between 0 and
1 Reward: Windsword

How to Complete: Talk to Jake.
He needs an Iron to complete his
sword. If you already have one
just give it to him. Otherwise
go to any dungeon and break the
mining stones until you find one
(it is a common mineral to find,
only loses to scrap iron). Just
a note, there is a bug that
might happen after you talk
again with Jake, he'll ask you
to bring a piece of Daikon
Radish, just ignore and give an
Iron. Return and deliver it to
him, receiving your reward.


Get Me Materials for Armor
--------------------------------
Description: I don't have enough
materials to make armor. If you
get some for me, I'll give ya
something good. Requirement:
Have completed Jake's first (2nd
generation) quest: "Get Me
    Swordmaking Materials"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: Greatsword

How to Complete: Talk to Jake.
He needs you to get a Tortoise
Shell to complete his armor
since his son is a little lazy.
If you already have one, you can
give it to him and finish the
quest right now. If you don't
have one, you can proceed to
Blessia Island - Altar/Old Ship
or Blessia Island - Sandy Path
(I suggest this place because
you can kill two of them at same
time) anytime and you'll find
Tortoises there. Defeat some of
them until they drop the
Tortoise Shell, pick it up and
give it to Jake. Look like he
can praise sometimes.


I've Got a Test for Ya
--------------------------------
Description: I'm interested in
yer sword-wielding skills. Come
here. Requirement: Have
completed Jake's second (2nd
generation) quest: "Get Me
    Materials for Armor"
Friendship Level: Between 4 and
5 Reward: Magical Lance

How to Complete: Talk to Jake.
He'll mention that your father
was a fairly "decent" warrior
and want to check your
potential. For this, Jake will
give you a special weapon just
made for you, so you can surpass
the skill of Kyle. Still
reading? Yeah, the quest is
over.

7.7.13. Leann's Quests
        [Leann-Q2]
================================

Looking for Someone to Talk to
--------------------------------
Description: I would like to
have a conversation with
someone. Requirement: Start
second generation Friendship
Level: 1 Reward: 2000G

How to Complete: Talk to Leann.
As the title says, she wants to
talk with someone about a
problem she's having. What kind
of problem a daughter of a rich
family can have? Keep talking to
her and Leann will asks some
tips to you (yeah, nobody is
perfect). Your character will
automatically say some answers
to her and she'll be happy with
your help, giving something to
you (and you won't accept, but
she is more skilled than you).


Some Casual Conversation
--------------------------------
Description: I would like to
talk to someone for a little
while. Requirement: Have
completed Leann's first quest:
"Looking for Someone to Talk
    to" and be playing as Aaron
Friendship and Love Level: 4
Reward: Leann as girlfriend?

How to Complete: Talk to Leann.
She wants to talk about another
problem and since you helped her
before she thinks you can help
her again. Now Leann will
explain that she has developed a
bad habit recently (omg, what
should it be?). She is walking
up in the middle of night and
snacking some junk foods. She
Will ask your opinion about that
and two options will appear.
Choose any option and the result
will be the same (what a shame,
poor Leann, calling her fat),
this will serve as incentive so
she can stop those night
snacking, but also Leann will
ask how do you fell about
slightly plump girls and you
will prove to her that you
like/love her in anyway she
looks like (and different from
other guys to Aria, Aaron is a
lot more aggressive towards the
girls). Two days will pass.

"Something's Bothering
 Me..." and be playing as Aria
Friendship and Love Level: 8

How to complete: Talk to Leonel.
There's something he has been
wanting to talk to you about.
Listen to what he has to say and
he will ask what you think of

answer "I like you... as a

abandoned, but you can start
again.

7.7.16. Max's Quests [Max-Q2]
================================

Conduct an Experiment (Big
Money!)
--------------------------------
Description: Work as an
assistant on an experiment
testing the strength of
    steel. Easy! Safe! Guarantee
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level:
Between 0 and 1 Reward: 15000G

How to Complete: Talk to Max. He
wants you to help him to measure
the strength of the steel that
he has developed. He'll give you
the steel, you need to hit with
your weapon and see how much
damage you do. To do that just
keep tapping the Touch Screen
with the Stylus until he tells
that is enough. After this Max
will say that the test was a
failure and give your payment
for the job. Actually you don't
need to do anything and you'll
be rewarded at the same way.
Note: I hit 27 times and he just
keep saying it was a failure, so
I can't say if something
different occurs with you hit
more than that.


Finish the Experiment (Big
Money!)
--------------------------------
Description: More work as an
assistant testing the strength
of steel. Easy!
    Safe! Guaranteed to be worth
Requirement: Have completed
Max's first (2nd generation)
quest: "Conduct an
    Experiment (Big Money!)"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: 30000G and Missing
Page 2 (Shine)

How to Complete: Talk to Max. He
wants to continue the previous
measure test today, like the
preceding quest just keep
tapping the Touch Screen with
the Stylus until he tells that
is enough. Exactly the same as
before, you can do nothing to
get the reward or you can do
what it was said. Another
failure, but work is work, so
take your payment from him.

7.7.18. Orland's Quests
        [Orland-Q2]
================================

Something for You
--------------------------------
Description: I have something to
give you. Come see me.
Requirement: Talk to him once.
Friendship Level: 0 (for Aaron)
/ Friendship and Love Level: 0
(for Aria) Reward: Spinach Seed

How to complete: Talk to Orland.
He'll give you a Spinach Seed.
Roy gave it to him but since he
doesn't need it (passing unlike
presents to others), it goes to
you. Orland will ask if you want
it or not, answer "I'll take it"
to get it immediately or answer
"I can't take it...". If you
choose the second option he'll
just toss it and ask again if
you don't want, answer "Don't
throw it away. I'll take it."
(if you answer again "I can't
take it..." he is going to do
exactly what he said).


A Message from the Teacher
--------------------------------
Description: I need to you to
run an errand for me.
Requirement: Have completed
Orland's first quest: "Something
for You" Friendship Level: 2
(for Aaron) / Friendship and
Love Level: 2 (for Aria) Reward:
100G

How to complete: Talk to Orland.
He needs you to deliver a Little
Crystal to Barrett (lazy boy).
Do this favor to him and give it
to your teacher Barrett. Go back
and inform him about Barrett's
complain, getting you great tip.


I Secretly Want Something
--------------------------------
Description: This is kind of a
secret request. Requirement:
Have completed Orland's second
quest: "A Message from the
Teacher"
    and be playing as Aria
Friendship and Love Level: 4
Reward: Cherry Grass Seed

How to complete: Talk to Orland.
He's a bit of an insect buff and
need you to take an Insect Jaw
to his collection. To find this
item, you need to wait until
night, then go to Messhina
Valley and kill Hornets or Queen
Bees (they drop the Insect Jaw).
I suggest you to go Messhina
Valley - Ruins because you can
find three Queen Bees at the
same map, but feel free to
choose another map (check
Monster Section to further
information). After you get one,
go back, give it to Orland,
listen some "thanks" and receive
your reward.


I Have a Request for You
--------------------------------
Description: Class has been too
easy lately and it's becoming a
problem. Requirement: Have
completed Orland's third quest:
"I Secretly Want Something"
    and be playing as Aria
Friendship and Love Level: 6
Reward: 200G

How to complete: Talk to Orland.
He isn't happy with his lessons
since it's too easy for him, so
he wants harder classes. Orland
wants you to go and talk to
Barrett to teach more difficult
lessons. So go, find Barrett and
talk to him about Orland's
complains (for your hope he will
only do more challenging lessons
to Orland and keep the regular
lessons to the rest of the
class). Now return and tell the
good news to Orland, see him
happy for a moment (this guy
even smile or is he just like
his father?) and receive a small
charge.


Just Come Over, Please
--------------------------------
Description: I need to talk to
you for a little. Requirement:
Have completed Orland's third
quest: "I Have a Request for
You"
    and be playing as Aria
Friendship and Love Level: 8
Reward: Orland as boyfriend?

How to complete: Talk to Orland.
He will ask a bunch of questions
about him and you also will make
some other questions. You will
discover some facts (like what
he thinks of you) and after some
more conversation he will ask if
you like him. If you answer "I
like you, Orland.", he'll be
happy and will take you to the
church to play of wedding, two
days will pass. But if you
answer "I like you as a friend,
Orland." the quest will be
abandoned, but you can start
again.


================================
7.7.19. Ray's Quests [Ray-Q2]
================================

Information for the Fitness Exam
--------------------------------
Description: I'm holding a
fitness examination. Your
participation would be
    much appreciated.
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level:
Between 2 and 3 Reward: Tomato
Juice (bad reward), Fruit Ole
(good reward) or Royal Curry
(very
    good reward) and Missing Pag

How to Complete: Talk to Ray. He
wants to test you with some
exercises. When he says "go",
just press the A Button as fast
as you can. After that Ray will
ask if you want to try again or
stop. If you don't like your
mark you can try again by
choosing to try again, otherwise
just choose to stop. If you
press the button very fast and
score a lot of hits (I'm not
sure about the exact value, I
think it's over 60), you'll
receive a Royal Curry as a
reward. Scoring over 40 hits,
gives you a Fruit Ole or, if you
do less than that, you'll
receive the Tomato Juice. But no
matter your score, you'll always
receive a Missing Page.


================================
7.7.20. Rosalind's Quests
        [Rosalind-Q2]
================================

Can You Get Me Some Food?
--------------------------------
Description: Could you please
get me a special kind of food?
(See me for
    details)
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 10000G

How to Complete: Talk to
Rosalind. She wants you to fish
a Salmon. I suggest you to try
to catch one in Messhina Valley
- Serene Garden, but you can go
anywhere you want, just check
the Fishing List section in this
guide. After you catch one go
back and deliver it to Rosalind
and get your tip.


Can You Get Something for Me?
--------------------------------
Description: Could you please
get something for me? (See me
for details) Requirement: Have
completed Rosalind's first (2nd
generation) quest: "Can You
    Get Me Some Food?"
Friendship Level: Between 2 and
3 Reward: 20000G

How to Complete: Talk to
Rosalind. She wants you to get
some Relax Tealeaves for her. To
complete this quest you need
first to have expanded your
school, built a workshop and
bought at least the small
kitchen station from Yue on
Mondays. To make the item (you
can learn this lesson on
Tuesday, at Difficult Cooking
topic) you need to collect the
following items: Blue Grass,
Green Grass, Medicinal Herb,
Purple Grass, White Grass,
Yellow Grass (all can be bought
at Alvarna Clinic) and cooking
level 26 (for success rate
100%), check the Cooking Section
for further details. After you
complete it, talk to Rosalind
and give her request.

7.7.21. Roy's Quests [Roy-Q2]
================================

I Lost Something in My House
--------------------------------
Description: I lost something in
my house... Come and help me
look for it. Requirement: Start
second generation Friendship
Level: 0 (for Aaron) /
Friendship and Love Level: 0
(for Aria) Reward: Rasin Bread

How to complete: Talk to Roy.
Distracted as always, he lost a
Pin that he borrowed from
Leonel. To help him to find it,
go to Sharper Edge Blacksmith
2F, walk all the way to the
north wall and them walk right.
In the corner press the A button
and you'll find the Pin behind
the lances. Give it to him and
take a food as reward.


Talk Some Sense into My Mom!
--------------------------------
Description: There's something
that I want you to say to my mom
for me. Requirement: Have
completed Roy's first (2nd
generation) quest: "I Lost
    Something in My House"
Friendship Level: 2 (for Aaron)
/ Friendship and Love Level: 2
(for Aria) Reward: Missing Page
1 (Sonic Wind)

How to complete: Talk to Roy. He
wants you to talk to his mother
since Tanya wants him to take
over the family business, but
Roy haven't decided what he
wanna do in the future, so he
needs you to explain that to
her. Find Tanya and start a
conversation. She'll understand
the situation and also ask you
if you want the job (she knows
what is the best for her). Go
back and inform the news to Roy
and finish the quest.


I'm Trying to Study
--------------------------------
Description: I was thinking of
studying but, of course, I'm no
good at it... Requirement: Have
completed Roy's second (2nd
generation) quest: "Talk Some
    Sense into My Mom!" and be p
Friendship and Love Level: 4
Reward: Salad

How to complete: Talk to Roy. He
has some troubles to understand
the lessons in school because he
can't concentrate, so maybe a
Hot Milk can help to improve it.
Since Roy can't remember how to
do it from the previous classes,
he'll give you a Small Milk, so
you can prepare it for him. So
go to Alvarna Academy -
Workshop, check the pot and warm
the milk (need cooking level 6
to have 100% of success rate).
You can also buy it from Yue for
1400G. After this go back and
deliver his order, receiving
your reward and seeing his
progress.


I Have a Secret Plan!
--------------------------------
Description: I have a secret
plan. Come and talk to me about
it. Requirement: Have completed
Roy's third (2nd generation)
quest: "I'm Trying to Study" and
be playing as Aria Friendship
and Love Level: 6 Reward: a
participation on a failed plan

How to complete: Talk to Roy. He
will be at Alvarna Academy -
Classroom and will explain his
secret plan, he wants to sneak
into school tonight. Roy will
convince you to go with him, so
meet him at Alvarna Academy at
PM 09:00. Start a conversation
and follow him (he made a secret
passage, but the doors are
always unlocked, so I don't know
why he did it), exploring the
school during night. After a
while Barrett will come and will
stop your playing. In the end
Roy and you will move out of the
school go home.


Come to My House
--------------------------------
Description: Come over. There's
something I want to talk to you
about. Requirement: Have
completed Roy's fourth (2nd
generation) quest: "I Have a
    Secret Plan!" and be playing
Friendship and Love Level: 8
Reward: Roy as boyfriend?

How to complete: Talk to Roy.
He'll say that he really like
you and will ask what do you
think about him. If you answer
"I like you too.", Roy'll take
you to church ask to marry (just
to play) with you and two days
will pass. But if you answer "I
like you as a friend, Roy." the
quest will be abandoned, but you
can start again.

7.7.22. Sera & Serena's Quests
        [Sera&Serena-Q2]
================================

Let's Play Hide-and-Seek!
--------------------------------
Description: Come play hide-and-
seek with us! Requirement: Talk
to them once. Friendship Level:
0 Reward: Marmalade

How to complete: Talk to Sera &
Serena. They'll invite you to
play hide-and-seek, so you need
to find them (they'll disappear
after you or they change the
map). They'll just keep moving
to different spots (I found them
at Alvarna - North Square next
where Yue stay in this map,
other time I found them walking
at De Sainte-coquille Park and
other at De Sainte-coquille
Dining Hall), so to remove all
doubts just cheat and ask to
Alicia to find them (the life
isn't always fair). Talk to them
and receive your prize. Sera &
Serena also tell that they love
this reward.


Come Play with Us!
--------------------------------
Description: We're looking for
someone to play with us!
Requirement: Have completed Sera
& Serena's first quest: "Let's
Play
    Hide-and-Seek!"
Friendship Level: 2
Reward: Chocolate Cookie

How to complete: Talk to Serena
(yes, only her) at Alvarna -
North Square. She'll explain
that she was playing hide-and-
seek with Sera, but can't find
her. Help Serena to find her
another half (too sad to see
only one of them). Go to Blessia
Island - Sandy Path and rescue
Sera there (Tortoises are still
in there). After talking to her
(for someone lost she has
courage to get back alone), go
meet them at Alvarna - North
Square and receive a half
present from Serena (Sera wants
the other half). Note: If you
start this quest and ask to
Alicia to locate the twins
(without meeting Serena before),
Sera will not be available to be
find anywhere, so Alicia says
she is Far-off City (like Yue
after AM 12:00).


Let's Play a Guessing Game!
--------------------------------
Description: We're looking for
someone to play with us!
Requirement: Have completed Sera
& Serena's second quest: "Come
Play with Us!" Friendship Level:
4 Reward: Pudding (right choice)
and Sardine Sashimi (wrong
choice)

How to complete: Talk to Sera &
Serena at Alvarna - North
Square. Sera will suggest to
play "Who's Who?" but will not
explain how to do that, so I'll
do that (as if someone really
need it, but anyway...). They
will start to walk in the same
place and after a while they
will ask who is Sera. Easy task,
if you pay attention at their
clothes, hair, you will see they
are pretty different. Sera have
the left eye uncover by her
hair, use her scarf at the right
side and have long sleeves with
a orange detail in the tip.
Serena have the right eye
uncover, use her scarf at the
left side and have a white cloth
at her shoulders.

To make this simple, the right
option is "Sera's on the left!"
and you will receive the best
prize. If you choose "Sera's on
the right!" Serena will say
you're wrong and Sera will ask
if you want to try again (if you
answer "No." the quest will be
abandoned, so you can redo
checking on the bulletin board
and if you answer "Sure!" they
will mix again). If you "I don't
have any idea!" the quest will
be over and you will get the
worst prize.


Something a Little More Grown Up
--------------------------------
Description: There's something
we've been wanting to do for a
while. Requirement: Have
completed Sera & Serena's third
quest: "Let's Play a Guessing
    Game!"
Friendship Level: 6 Reward: Sera
& Serena as girlfriends?

How to complete: Talk to Sera &
Serena. Serena will ask if you
like her (and after that Sera
will ask the same). If you
answer "No, not really..." for
one of them the quest will be
abandoned (you can start again
if you want), so answer "I like
you." to them both. Now they
will ask you to bring them the
Stoller Chalice and say to get
more information from Leann.
Meet her and she will explain
the story behind it, also
telling that her father Max have
bought it. Leann accept to
borrow it to you, so go to De
Sainte-coquille Dinning Hall and
walk straight to the wall in
front of the door's entrance to
find it. Now go meet Sera &
Serena, giving the Stoller
Chalice to them. Now they want
you to propose to them. After
that a day will pass.

7.7.23. Tanya's Quests
        [Tanya-Q2]
================================

Trial!: Pomme Pomme
--------------------------------
Description: Want to try some
training? Come see me,'kay?
Quest Can Be Replayed
Requirement: Start second
generation Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 500G

How to Complete: Talk to Tanya.
She'll tell how good was Kyle at
fighting (exaggerating a
little), starting to claim you
need to become a skilled fighter
as well. So that is the plan,
Tanya will introduce you to a
lot of different trials, you
need to complete them all,
becoming more and more strong.
To start, she'll ask you to head
to Trieste Forest - Spring
Clearing and defeat 10 Pomme
Pommes. They'll be only
available at day time and there
are two of them in the map.
After completing this easy task,
go back and take your prize.


Trial!: Orc
--------------------------------
Description: Time for training!
Come see me, 'kay? Quest Can Be
Replayed Requirement: Have
completed Tanya's first (2nd
generation) quest: "Trial!:
    Pomme Pomme"
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 600G

How to Complete: Talk to Tanya.
This time your target will be 10
Orcs. Proceed to Trieste Forest.
They can be found on Trieste
Forest - Grassy Path and Trieste
Forest - Windy Pass (north
entrance) during day, that is,
before PM 06:00. There is one
Gate that spawn the Orc in
Grassy Path, so if you think
it's annoying to fight against
two monsters at the same time,
try to destroy the north Gate,
so that only one will keep
respawning Orc. In Windy Pass
there is one Gate that spawns 2
Orcs, so it's the best place to
complete this quest. After
killing 10 Orcs, go back and
take your prize.


Trial!: Ants
--------------------------------
Description: Time for training!
Come see me, 'kay? Quest Can Be
Replayed Requirement: Have
completed Tanya's second (2nd
generation) quest: "Trial!:
    Orc"
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 500G

How to Complete: Talk to Tanya.
This time your target will be 10
Ants. Proceed to Trieste Forest
- Aegis Falls during night
(after PM 06:00). There are two
Gates in this map, the left one
spawns 2 Ants and the right one
spawns only 1. After killing 10
Ants, go back and take your
prize.


Trial!: Flower Blossom
--------------------------------
Description: Time for training!
Come see me, 'kay? Quest Can Be
Replayed Requirement: Have
completed Tanya's third (2nd
generation) quest: "Trial!:
    Ants"
Friendship Level: 0
Reward: 500G

How to Complete: Talk to Tanya.
This time your target will be 10
Flower Blossoms. Proceed to
Trieste Forest. They can be
found on Trieste Forest - Grassy
Path or Trieste Forest - Sun-
Dapplet Spot. In Grassy Path
there are two Gates, one that
spawns Orcs and the other that
spawns the Flower Blossom.
Destroy the right Gate and kill
the Orc, so you can concentrate
only in the Flower Blossom. You
can go in this map anytime. In
Trieste Forest - Sun-Dapplet
Spot you can only find the
target monster at daytime and
there is one Gate that spawns
Flower Blossom and Orc Hunter.
To respawn you need to kill them
both, so I suggest you to go to
Trieste Forest - Grassy Path.
After killing 10 Flowers
Blossoms, go back and take your
prize.

Island - West Beach since both
Gates spawns Blood Panthers, but
if that is too much just destroy
one of them. After killing 20
Blood Panthers, go back and take
your prize.

7.7.24. Yue's Quests [Yue-Q2]
================================

I Got Something Good
--------------------------------
Description: I've got somethin'
for you. Come 'round and see me
for it. Requirement: Start
second generation Friendship
Level: 0 Reward: Missing Page 1
(Medication)

How to Complete: Talk to Yue.
Good as always, she'll give you
a present for free (maybe she
can't forget her love about
Kyle...) since it doesn't have a
use for her. Simple quest, it
would be easier if you just had
to talk to Yue instead of
starting a new quest.


Again, I Got Something Good
--------------------------------
Description: I got my hands on
it again. Come by if you want
it. Requirement: Have completed
Yue's first quest: "I Got
Something Good" Friendship
Level: Between 2 and 3 Reward:
Missing Page 1 (Life Drain)

How to Complete: Talk to Yue.
Same as the previous quest. Just
talk to Yue and she will give
you another piece of Missing
Page.


Once Again, I Got Something Good
--------------------------------
Description: I managed to get it
one more time. Come get it! I'll
be waitin'! Requirement: Have
completed Yue's second quest:
"Again, I Got Something Good"
Friendship Level: Between 4 and
5 Reward: Missing Page 1 (Shine)

How to Complete: Same as always.
Talk to her and receive another
Missing Page.


********************************
7.8. Festivals [Festivals]
********************************

Festivals are a good opportunity
to increase friendship level
with the villagers, as talking
and giving gifts to them in
these dates have a stronger
effect on the friendship level
than usual days. Besides, you
can also enjoy the mini games in
the festivals and obtain prizes
from them as well as increase
friendship even more.

One interesting note about
festivals days is that it'll
never rain in these days, even
if you pay Alicia to do so.

Everybody is in a fixed position
over the map in festival days,
the table below shows where you
can find everybody (depending on
the festival they can change
they're positions, but if that
happens I'll tell where they'll
be instead):


 Villager Name | Location       
--------------------------------
 Alicia        | Alvarna - North
 Barrett.......|.Alvarna - Falli
 Byron         | De Sainte-coqui
 Cammy.........|.Alvarna - East 
 Cecilia       | Alvarna - North
 Dorothy.......|.Alvarna - Falli
 Douglas       | Alvarna Clinic 
 Egan..........|.Alvarna - East 
 Gordon        | Alvarna Clinic 
 Herman........|.De Sainte-coqui
 Jake          | Alvarna - Falli
 Julia.........|.Alvarna - Port.
 Leann         | Alvarna Academy
 Leonel........|.Alvarna Academy
 Mana          | Alvarna - North
 Max...........|.Alvarna - Port 
 Natalie       | Alvarna Clinic 
 Orland........|.Alvarna Academy
 Ray           | Alvarna - West 
 Rosalind......|.Alvarna - West 
 Roy           | Alvarna - East 
 Sera & Serena.|.Alvarna Academy
 Tanya         | Alvarna - Port 
 Yue...........|.Alvarna - Pond.

Note: When it start to becoming
dark all the villagers move to
their respective homes. Also,
after a couple get married they
won't appear anymore at the
festivals, they will spend all
day inside their house.
** In second generation all marr
(except Cecilia and Mana/Alicia
if they're your mother, they go
to De Sainte-coquille Park after
AM 09:00) and married guys will
come back to their original
places.

Below you'll see about the
festivals in this game. They'll
follow the model shown just
below:


Date - Festival Name
--------------------------------
Brief description of what's the
main idea of this festival.


Notes about this festival What
you should do in this festival.


Spring 1 - New Year's Day
--------------------------------
The first festival of the year
and the last festival you see
(since you only arrive in
Alvarna one day after it). A new
Year has come! Everything renews
in this day. Start to think your
plans for this year and prepare
for more work to do! Happy New
Year!


Notes about this festival No
special comments about this
festival. Everybody is in the
standard position and they only
say something about this day.
Just do your daily tasks as
usual.


Spring 13 - Flower Festival
--------------------------------
In this day of year, colored
papers are falling from the sky
in the city (like all the others
festivals). Some villagers are
talking about how beautiful
flowers are, other just want to
use the festival as an excuse to
drink in the afternoon (as Jake
say), and you can invite girls
to see the cherry blossoms under
the cherry tree and raise their
affections. Each girl make a
comment about a fact in her
life. If you want invite them
all (need to reset the game) to
see what they say (I decided to
not write about what they say
since it is better you to see
than read and also because I'm
lazy).


Notes about this festival Ok,
for know some things you should
know about this festival.
- Everybody is in the standard p
- You can invite any romantic in
- Walk to Cherry Blossom Square 
- Only the first three will acce
 second generation you can invit
- If you try to invite the other
 been with someone else and thei
 one level if you have just rais

I suggest to choose the girls
you like the most or the ones
who have the lowest love level
at the moment (for example
Rosalind, Alicia in the first
year since it is difficult to
get their favorite presents in
this time). For second
generation just invite everyone!


Spring 25 - Eating Contest
Festival
--------------------------------
As one of the most primitive
instincts of the humans, in this
festival you will eat as much as
possible to win the contest.
This is the most waited day for
Herman, so he can to show his
amazing abilities and do a
perfect judgment of the
tournament (or at least only to
see he isn't the only one who
can eat a lot). Some girls will
cheer for you to win the contest
(do they like a fluffy man?).


Notes about this festival
- Characters in different places
 of your house, Douglas and Gord
 Ray (second generation) will be
- Talk to Herman to start the co
 until 5:30 PM.
- When he says "Start!", press t
 until he says "Stop!".
- The rewards are:
    * Grand Prize (1st place) ge
  Formula A (first generation) /
    * Honorable Mention (2nd pla
  Pizza (second generation);
    * Consolation Prize (3rd pla
  (second generation).

If you want to win you need to
get at least 35 bites. Winning
will increase everybody
friendship and love points.


Summer 1 - 1st Day of Summer
--------------------------------
Finally the first day of summer!
The hot season which everyone
was waiting, mostly the kids,
since now everybody can swim.
The girls will say that they can
ready their swimsuits in the day
before it, so it's time for a
true man enjoy his life after a
long time working. Take a deep
breath, get out of your house
and meet the girls in the city
with their... daily clothes?
Yeah... that's all, they know
how to break a man's heart...


Notes about this festival There
isn't too much to comment about
this festival, it's just a
festival day without anything
particular, all villagers will
be at their fixed positions on
festival day and you don't need
to do nothing different the
usual. Boring day, very boring
day.


Summer 7 - Monster Taming
Festival
--------------------------------
A special day to strengthen and
get strengthen the ties between
humans (and some elves) and
monsters. With a brave and kind
heart, show your taming skill
(as Cecilia said: "You seen like
the type of person who is meant
to tame the land and its
monsters.") as the Earthmate
Master, impressing everyone in
town. To do that, follow the
below instruction.


Notes about this festival
- Characters in different places
 of your house, Max and Jake (fi
 (second generation) will be in 
- You need to complete Cecilia's
 the item Pet Glove, essential t
- You need at least a barn and o
- Talk to Herman to start the co
 until 5:30 PM.
- This contest is a competition 
 specific monster, Herman will a
  to catch a specific monster.
- The rewards are:
    * Grand Prize (1st place) ge
  Formula B (first generation)/ 
  (second generation);
    * Honorable Mention (2nd pla
  Union Stew (second generation)
    * Consolation Prize (3rd pla
  Eggplant (second generation).

Note: At least in my version of
game there is a bug in this
festival. If you want to win
this festival you need to catch
the monsters before the hour
counter in the internal clock of
the game changes. For example if
you talk to Herman at 8:XX you
need to catch the monster before
it turns 9:00, so I suggest you
to start this contest at the
first minutes of a new hours (if
you talk to Herman at X:59 and
don't use cheat or glitch you'll
automatically lose the 1st
place, as it's impossible to
tame a monster in less than 1
minute).


Summer 19 - Dance Festival
--------------------------------
Time to take a break and forget
all your hard work. This
festival is a good opportunity
to ask your favorite girl out to
a dance and show that you can be
more than a farmer (or
adventurer, or blacksmith, or
hunter, or whatever you are) and
impress her with your amazing
moves (better than some of
previous games) with a warm
music in the background. In my
opinion, everybody should stay
in the same place to see the
couples dancing, somewhere
beautiful like the Cherry
Blossom Square, but probably
that would lag a lot, so sad...


Notes about this festival
- Everybody is in the standard p
- You can only dance with potent
  with Love Level 4 or above.
- You can dance only with one gi

I suggest to choose the
character you most like or who
have the lowest love level at
the moment.


Summer 25 - Fishing Contest (1st
generation) / Big Cook-Off (2nd
generation)
--------------------------------
Fishing is the perfect sport to
relax in a sunny and comfortable
day of summer (at least for some
people). For others "Fishing is
a fierce, heroic battle. A match
between person and fish. A
gladiatorial contest where your
wits will earn you glorious
victory or crushing defeat." as
Rosalind said. If you want to
dedicate to such a finest art
you need a lot of concentration,
a good bait and years of
training to develop your own
technique. But I trust in the
main character abilities, since
he/she can fish a completely
polished stone with a rod as I,
personally, would never be able
to do the same. In the second
generation this festival will be
changed to a Cook Contest, so

Fall 13 - Harvest Festival
--------------------------------
A traditional festival in
Harvest Moon series. This day
everybody celebrates and shows
your grateful for the gifts of
the land, our daily food. As a
farmer, it is your duty to give
a special thanks for the grace
of the soil that we are able to
keep farming. Some villagers
also comments how delicious is
the vegetables from your farm
and praises for your hard work.


Notes about this festival No
special comments about this
festival. Everybody is in the
standard position and they only
say something about this day.
Just do your daily tasks as
normal.


Fall 25 - Monster Contest
--------------------------------
After you win the title of
"Monster Master" at the Monster
Taming Festival, it is your
destiny to get the other title
of "Monster Master", but now in
Monster Contest. An alliance
between humans and monsters
don't end after you manage to
tame one, but only after you get
more close this ties, with much
affection and training every
single day (and many more
brushes), raising the trust of
this two different races. Bring
your best friend (the most
powerful in this case) to the
contest and get another prize to
your collection (not a very
important one, but still a
prize).

Winter 30 - New Year's Eve
--------------------------------
A long year has passed. Time to
think what you have done for
this entire year and check your
goals for the next one. Walk
down the street, listen the last
words of the year, remembering
the good (sometimes bad) moments
with all villagers and
everything you received in this
friendly town called Alvarna.
Best wishes for the coming year
to everybody.

special comments about this

standard position and they only
say something about this day.
Just do your daily tasks as
normal.


********************************
7.9. Villagers [Villagers]
********************************

In this section you'll find some
info about the villagers in this
game. The subsections include
what gift you can give him/her
to increase (or decrease) the
friendship level, when is
his/her birthday and finally a
brief section about the
bachelorettes you can marry in
the first generation.

To enter freely at people's
house you need to have at least
Friendship Level 3 with the
ownership of the place.


================================
7.9.1. Villager Likes/Dislike
       [Likes]
================================

Here you'll see what each
villager like/dislike and
therefore what you can give
him/her as a gift if you want to
increase/decrease his/her
Friendship Level.

Notice that you can only give
one present a day for each
person. Giving a lot of them in
the same day doesn't change
anything and it'll be a waste.
Additionally, be careful when
giving the gifts, see if you're
really giving only one unit of
the item and not a group of
them, as this too is not
different than giving only one
unit.

================================
7.9.4. Schedule - Second
       Generation [Schedule2]
================================

In second generation, new
characters will appear in the
story and all people will have a
new different routine In the
particular case of your mother,
she'll have the same schedule
below except that when you can't
find her, she will be at your
home. So these are their new
schedule (also note the same
rules used in the previous
section will be use in this
one):

================================
7.9.5. Bachelorettes - First
       Generation
       [Bachelorettes]
================================

About Marriage: If you want to
get married, you need to raise
the Love Level of the girl you
want to marriage up to 10 and
give the proposal item to her
(if you complete all the
requirements, you can ask her in
marriage at any moment, include
in festivals day). Also you can
wait until the default wedding
day of the girl you like and
confess to her during the
ceremony (yes, you can steal the
fiance, but only works if you
don't have married with another
girl and have her Love Level
10), but your friendship with
her ex-partner will drop. Don't
work with Alicia, Mana and Yue
as they don't have a default
marriage. Also when you give to
her the Proposal Item, the
wedding will automatically start
in the next day (so do all your
daily tasks before that). After
the ceremony, another day will
pass and both of you will start
the day at your home. You lose a
entire day at other villagers
weddings days (if you go to the
bed in a wedding day it you
occurs at the day you try to
move out of your house).

================================
7.9.6. Love Candidates - Second
       Generation [Love]
================================

As the main character in the
second generation part of the
game isn't a fully grown person
yet, he/she cannot get married
at his/her age, but that doesn't
mean he/she can't date and have
a celebration with the special
someone he/she likes.

Because there's no actual
marriage, opposite from before,
as a child you can "marry" as
many candidates you want (once
each, obviously) and don't need
to worry about losing quests
from others or anything like
that. The "marriages" also don't
have proposal items, the
celebration will always be
triggered by the last quest of
the candidate. All you need to
do is to take the quest and,
after talking to the requester,
answer whether you really like
him/her or not. In the negative
case, nothing really happens and
you can take the quest again, if
you want. On the other hand, if
you say you do like him/her,
you'll be in the church in the
next day and a marriage will
occur the same as it happened in
the first generation, except
that no one talks to you after
the event and you won't live
together. In fact, after the
event, everybody will act as if
nothing happened at all and
nothing will change.

About the candidates. As you can
choose if you want to be a male
or female character in the
second generation, obviously
there are candidates for both
genres. I'll list below the
possible choices, starting by
the girls and then the boys.

--------------------------------

the first generation. Somehow

################################
8. Monsters                     
################################

The monster are assumed to be on
Friendship Level 0.

Every monster is a Fighting-Type
monster implicitly, so when I
say a monster is, for example, a
Farming-Type monster I actually
mean he's a Farming-Type AND a
Fighting-Type monster. On the
other hand, when I say a monster
is a Fighting- Type monster that
means he's ONLY a Fighting-Type
and can't help you on your farm
or produce anything.

The produce cycle from Produce
Type monster is 3 days after you
capture it (except Wolly, which
you can take small fleece just
after capturing one), that means
every 3 days you can gather the
productions from them.

Also the Produce-Type Monster
will produce item at low quality
while friendship Level is
between 0 - 3, medium quality
between 4 - 7 and high quality
between
8 - 10

The first table below shows the
basic model of how the monster
info is disposed:

Monster Name
--------------------------------
Description: The info you can
see in the game about the
monster Found in: What dungeon
you can find this monster (time
of the day it'll appear:
    Day, Night or Anytime)
Monster Type: What it can do
(farm, fight, produce or ride)
Item Dropped: The item you can
obtain by defeating this monster
HP: Health Points at level 0
Skill: The name of its attack
Attribute: Elemental attribute
of this monster Pet Counter: How
many pets you need to capture it

The time is counted as follows:
- Day: From AM 6:00 to PM 6:00
- Night: From PM 6:00 until you 
- Anytime: Both Day and Night

* Second generation only
