********************************
8.1. Monster Taming [Taming]
********************************

In this game, you're allowed to
tame the monsters you find in
the dungeons and this way you
can, besides collecting them,
tame monsters that can help on
your farm activities (harvest
and watering) or that can
produce goods for selling (eggs,
milk, wool, etc.). Notice all of
the monsters also can accompany
when you go to dungeons and
fight by your side against other
monsters.

Before you start to tame
monsters, you'll have to build a
barn in the village, so that the
new tamed monsters can live
there. You can do this by
talking to the mayor after
completing Cecilia's first quest
("Please Find Something") and
receiving the Pet Glove. If you
want to build the barn you'll
need 5000G and 50 pieces of
wood.

In order to be able to tame
monsters, you'll need the Pet
Glove, received from Cecilia
after you complete her first
quest. After you put your hands
in this glove, you'll be able to
tame monsters by equipping the
glove and then petting the
monsters in the dungeons with
it. Notice the monsters will
still attack you while you try
to pet them. In order to finish
the taming, keep petting the
monster until the a new window
appears asking for you to give a
name for your new partner.

*Each pet only counts if some he
likes you more.

The info about the pet glove is
just below:


Pet Glove
--------------------------------
What is it for: Taming wild
monsters to help you. How to
get: Reward from Cecilia after
finishing the quest "Please Find
    Something".
Description: Gloves that tell
your monsters you truly care.
Now you can laugh off those
loving nips and bites.


********************************
8.2. Monster Care [Care]
********************************

After you tame a monster, it's
important to take good care of
it. By doing so, you'll be
rewarded by being able to
collect better productions from
them and increasing their
fighting abilities. So, just to
make it clear, by taking good
care of your monsters, you'll
increase their friendship level
toward you and, by doing so,
you'll not only increase their
status (HP, Attack, etc.) but
also that will make them produce
higher quality (bigger) items
that are worth more.

So, what should you do to take
care of monsters? Well, first of
all, you need to feed them
everyday. Not doing so will
cause its friendship level to
fall (it won't die or anything,
don't worry). If you want to
feed a monster, all you need to
do is to get some Feed (an item)
and toss it in the hole outside
the barn. You can toss a lot of
feed at once, you don't need to
do this every day. Each monster
in the barn will eat one Feed a
day automatically, you just need
to make sure there is enough
food in the barn for all of
them. You can see how much feed
there is by reading the sign
just outside the barn.

You can get Feed in two ways:
you can buy it from Douglas for
400G each (very expensive!), or
you can buy some grass seeds and
plant them in your farm, wait
for they to grow and cut them
with your sickle. The latter is
a much better option, so I'd
recommend you to start planting
grass as soon as possible if you
want to tame some monsters. You
won't need to plant a lot of
grass at all. After it grows
once, you can cut it to collect
Feed and, after that, they'll
regrow in three days again,
allowing you to collect again.
This cycle is always repeated,
so you won't need to buy more
grass seeds each time you cut
them. Just DON'T CUT THE GRASS
TWICE IN A ROW, that is, before
it regrows because, by doing
this, you'll really kill the
grass and you'll need to plant
them again. Notice each tile of
grass you cut generates 4 Feed,
what means that if you cut a 3x3
area of grass you'll obtain 36
Feeds, not only 9 so, since the
grass regrows each 3 days, one
single 3x3 area of grass allows
you to feed 36 / 3 = 12 monsters
forever, as long as you keep the
grass regrowing. Notice as well
that, after you cut the grass,
it'll go to the barn and become
Feed automatically, so all you
need to do is to cut it in your
farm and don't need to toss them
in the hole of the barn.

Now retaking the care of
monsters point, besides feeding
them, it's important to brush
them everyday to make them
happier as well. This isn't
necessary at all and won't
affect their happiness if you
don't do this, but doing so you
increase their friendship much
faster. You can do this by
equipping your brush (see below
how to get it) and pressing the
tools button next to a monster.

Finally, I'll list below the
caring tools you can obtain and
what they're for, how you can
get them and the description
about them you can see in the
game:


Brush
--------------------------------
What is it for: Brushing your
monsters and increase their
friendship level. How to get:
Reward from Cecilia after
finishing the quest "Looking for
Special
    Ingredients"
Description: An item used when
caring for monsters. Stiff and
strong, capable
    of grooming even the coarses


Clippers
--------------------------------
What is it for: Cutting fleece
from tamed Woolies. How to get:
Reward from Egan after finishing
the quest "Please Taste This for
    Me"
Description: Used to trim and
clip monster fur. Designed so
that it is
    impossible to cut or hurt th


Harvest Basket
--------------------------------
What is it for: Collecting honey
(second generation only) from
tamed Hornets,
    Queen Bees or eggs from Cluc
How to get: Reward from Rosalind
after finishing the quest
"Please Find Me an
    Apple"
Description: An item used when
caring for and gathering from
monsters. Allows honey and eggs
to be collected.


Milker
--------------------------------
What is it for: Collecting milk
from tamed Buffamoos. How to
get: Reward from Herman after
finishing the quest "A Request
for
    Breakfast".
Description: Used to obtain milk
from a Buffamoo. Allows you to
collect their
    very nutritious milk.


********************************
8.3. Bosses                     
********************************

In the second generation, each
dungeon will have a guardian
boss at the last map you could
access as Kyle. To collect all
Tablet Fragments and open new
weapons at Tanya's store, it's
indispensable to defeat them
all. In this section I will
explain to you all move sets
from each boss and how to defeat
them. After taking down a lot
the boss hp, it will enter in a
berserk/near death state and
change its colors and new
attacks will come.

You need to kill them in the
season order (first killing the
spring guardian, and then the
summer guardian and so on),
because the next boss will not
appear until you defeat the
previous one. Also you need to
fight alone (no monster pet can
go with you) Also note, the name
of attacks is only based in what
I see, so none of them are
official.

I started to try to kill the
spring boss at level 10 and
proceeded until the winter boss
at level 20 so it's possible to
defeat them at a low level but
it can be a little difficult
since some attacks can kill you
in one hit (also all damage from
attacks are based in these low
level, what means that, at a
higher level the same attacks
can do damages close to 1). For
the secret bosses I start to
kill the first one at level 30.

The only weapon I really don't
recommend are hammers since
bosses don't take knock back and
the critical from an axe is a
lot of better. Longswords have a
long delay and take more time to
make 2 moves and axes can do a
great damage in critical but
have a delay to start and do an
average damage in normal hits.
If you're not good enough to
avoid most of attacks try to use
sword and shield to raise your
defense. I recommend spears the
most, so you can attack from a
safe distance and do a good
damage or shortswords since the
delay of each attack is really
short, except the last move
since it opens your guard for a
great amount of time, so pay
attention. About rods you can
use the spells from a safe
distance and attack when the
boss open its guard, but it can
be a little more difficult to
aim and you will normally have
only one chance to attack in
each opening. Since my magic
level was too low I didn't use
any spells to defeat the bosses.

For all bosses you can bring
potions to recover HP and
Invinciroid/Formuade (choose
only one of them, they cancel
each other), so you can give a
good boost in your stats for the
battle. Also check the Boss
attribute and create the best
equips (see Forging Section for
further informations) against
it.

*HP values are an approximation.


Trieste Forest Dungeon Guardian
- Terror Tree
--------------------------------
HP: 1000 Berserk Mode: 250 HP
left Attribute: Earth (Use wind
type attacks for extra damage)

Attack List:

- Root Spike: The boss raises bo
 in this move. Roots will grow u
 can also stuns you. This attack
- Swing Attack: Raises right arm
 damage (the most powerful from 
- Apples Falls: Put both hands t
 line of apples will appear from
 attack repeats 3 times in a row
- Circle of Apples: The boss wil
 eyes turns red. Eight apples wi
 into you. Low damage.
- Cure: Embrace itself and recov
- Rush: Berserk Attack Type. Aft
 your direction and stop for a f
 Continuous attack and low damag

Strategy:

As soon as you regain the
character control, just keep
running in the map to avoid the
Root Spike Attack. After that,
run and try to go behind the
boss from any side and attack
from this spot. Any weapon
should work well in this boss as
he can't move. Even if it tries
the Swing Attack, this spot is
out from its range, so just keep
attacking. It will also try to
attack you with Apples Falls,
try to avoid 3 times by walking
to right/left or just take the
hit, as it only inflicts little
damage. If it attacks with
Circle of Apples, you can choose
to take the damages or try to
move to the middle of the map
and avoid them by walking to the
sides. After avoiding (or taking
damage) just return to the
safety spot and attack again,
repeating the cycle. When its HP
goes low and it turns purple,
the boss will start the Rush
attack, you can avoid this and
hit 2 times its back, avoid
again and keep doing this until
you finally kill it.


Blessia Island Dungeon Guardian
- Octopirate
--------------------------------
HP: 1500 Berserk Mode: 380 HP
left Attribute: Fire (Use water
type attacks for extra damage)

Attack List:

- Spike Balls: A spike ball will
 this in you. It flies toward yo
 crossing half of the map distan
- Thrust: The Octopirate will mo
 its tentacles. Can inflict 4 hi
 faster and follow you. Low dama
- Spear Attack: It will raise it
 it will attack you 3 times, if 
 the same quantity of damage you
- Barrel Throw: It will raise it
 eyes will turn yellow and it'll
 direction that explode with the
 barrel) and repeat this attack 
- Tentacle Swing: Raise the midd
 stun. Low damage.
- Smoke Attack: Berserk Attack T
 spit a lot of little black smok
 take a lot of them if you stay 

Strategy:

First avoid the Spike Balls by
just getting out of his vision.
After an attack, the Octopirate
will come with a Thrust, so it
will always follow this sequence
of moves (a random attack,
thrust, random attack,
thrust...), try to attack as
much as you can when it's in the
middle of a thrust attack
(shortswords are highly
recommended) and always attack
from its sides (behind attacks
don't have effect because of its
hard shell and front attacks are
too dangerous). If you see it
preparing a Barrel Throw, take a
distance from it and try to run
to any side, avoiding the
barrels, and pay attention to
the explosions (it can still
damage you). In the case you see
it preparing a Spear Attack just
run to its side and attack. Keep
fighting until it enters in
berserk mode. When it turns all
red, stay close and get out of
the front its face (try to stay
exactly at its side. After the
it uses the smoke attack, try to
hit it twice and then wait it
turns to you and then move to
its side again. Repeat it until
you kill the Octopirate.


Messhina Valley Dungeon Guardian
- Bane Dragon
--------------------------------
HP: 2000 Berserk Mode: 500 HP
left Attribute: Wind (Use earth
type attacks for extra damage)

Attack list:

- Tongue Whip: The boss shakes i
 damage but causes paralysis (ve
- Rush: It will move back one st
 10 squares). Medium to high dam
- Energy Balls: Eyes turn blue. 
 its mouth and will come in zigz
- Vanish: When you and the Bane 
 the map.
- Seal Blow: It will come after 
 its eyes will turn blue, and it
 Medium to high damage (depends 
- Body Smashing: After a Seal Bl
 orange and it jumps in the same
 dead end (after Seal Blow) caus
 it. In Berserk Mode, it will al
 damage.

Strategy:

Run all the bridge until near
the end (pay attention to not
run towards it during the Rush
Attack). Now you have two ways
to defeat it:

- First Way: When you see it pre
the Bane Dragon near the point
where it stops (near 10 squares
of distance). Always attack two
times (use the max range of the
weapon when doing this) and
prepare for the next attack
hint. If you see it preparing
Tongue Whip, just run until you
can't see its face and
counterattack. If you see an
Energy Balls attack coming, you
can move the same amount of
space you would if you were to
avoid a rush attack and then
come back to see the next attack
(don't have enough time for a
counterattack) or stay 2 squares
away from its mouth, wait the
ball to move and walk in its
direction to avoid the ball and
repeat the process 2 more times
(need a good timing to do this)
and then attack twice. When you
reach the dead end with the Bane
Dragon, it will vanish and
appear from left or right, when
you see it, move to the other
side. After the attack, move
away from the dead end, wait the
Body Smashing and attack twice.

Repeat all the process again
until it gets in Berserk Mode.
Now the boss will only use Rush
and Body Smashing, Rush and Body
Smashing during all the bridge.
After a Rush, attack it once,
run to avoid the Body Smashing,
go back, attack twice, run to
avoid Rush, repeat the process
until you reach the dead end.
Use the dead end tactic and keep
doing this until you finally
kill it.

- Second Way: The easiest way to
to the dead end and wait the
boss reaches there. It will
Vanish and use the Seal Blow. As
the first way, run to the other
side from where it appears and,
after the attack, turn your back
in the dead end direction (stay
close it) and when you see the
boss jumping, start a complete
combo of your weapon as soon as
it touches the ground (you won't
get hit by the impact). Move
back to avoid the second Body
Smashing and repeat the cycle
until you can't do a complete
combo (it'll turn back faster
and if you keep doing this
tactic you won't ever kill the
boss). This time after the Seal
Blow, it'll run to the opposite
side of the dead end and enter
in Berserk Mode. Lure the Giant
Lizard to the other dead end and
repeat the process again until
you finally kill it for all.

Also note you can combine the
both ways, so you don't need to
wait and lure the boss to the
dead end.


Padova Mountains Dungeon
Guardian - Crystal Mammoth
--------------------------------
HP: 2501 Berserk Mode: 626 HP
left Attribute: Water (Use fire
type attacks for extra damage)

Attack List:

- Rush: It will face toward your
 In Berserk Mode it will move fa
 (depends on how many hits you t
 take a lot of hits.
- Snout Swing: Moves its body to
 in front of its face. High dama
- Crystal Barriers: When all cry
 Crystal Mammoth will raise its 
 barrier will appear from the gr
 (can do a one hit K.O. in low l
- Body Smashing: Berserk Attack 
 in the ground. The impact can c
- Vacuuming: Berserk Attack Type
 After that the Crystal Mammoth 

Strategy:

Dodge the first Rush attack and
stay close to it. You can do
this anywhere, but I suggest to
lure the Crystal Mammoth to the
center of the map, this way is
much easier to avoid his Snout
Swing than from the corners.
After the Rush attack wait the
Snout Swing hint, move to its
left side and do a complete
combo with your weapon if you
can. Wait again the Snout Swing
attack, attack again, repeat all
the cycle. Keep doing this
tactic, moving around it
(counterclockwise). When you see
all crystals in its back
shining, starts to pay
attention. The Crystal Mammoth
will raise its snout and prepare
the Crystal Barriers. Stay away
from it and wait until the
barriers starts to disappear.
Get closer and start the cycle
again (avoid the Snout Swing and
do a complete combo...). When it
enters in Berserk Mode, run away
from the Rush Attack and then
try to come closer. The Crystal
Mammoth will try a Body
Smashing, run away (but don't go
too far), go back and attack
once with a shortsword (the
delay of other weapons can be
too long, but you can try if you
want). It will try the same
attack again, so just keep
running and attacking once.
Maybe in a certain moment you'll
see your actions will be a
little slower than its attack,
so just wait two attacks from it
and get the timing again. Be
extremely careful, one hit from
a Body Smashing can stun you and
open your guard to a complete
Rush Attack and that can mean
your death. If you get too far
away from it, it will try to
Rush again in your direction or
use the Vacuuming (in this case
just run for the opposite side).
Wait until it stops and try to
come closer again. Continue the
hit-and-run tactic until you
kill it.


Palermo Shrine Dungeon Guardian
- Fiersome
--------------------------------
HP: 3000 Berserk Mode: 750 HP
left Attribute: Fire (Use water
type attacks for extra damage)

Attack List:

- Stomp: Fiersome starts to fly,
 fall down. Only the yellow fire
 can cause stun. In Berserk Mode
  the ground and move forward.
- Triple Fireball: It will raise
 your direction and can change t
 damage.
- Fireball Vacuum: Shakes its he
 absorbs giant fireballs from an
- Spin Attack: Fiersome raises i
high damage and can cause stun.
- Fireball Tornado: Berserk Atta
 (one opposite to another) and s
 very high damage (depends on ho
 instant kill if you are in a lo
- Homing Fireball: Berserk Attac
 aiming wherever you go. Shoots 
 Medium to high damage.


Strategy:

For this fight come prepared
with Icifier (level 10) or a
better shortsword if you can
(need to have a lot of more
attack since Icifier has the
water element advantage), and
some strong potions or Cure
magic book completely restored.
I fought with Fiersome at level
26, so it's possible to kill it
(but some attacks kill me
instantly, so maybe you need
some tries until you can finish
it). Now use Dragon Break as
soon as the fight start (it will
decrease his defense and
attack), wait Fiersome to fly
over your head, run to a medium
distance to avoid the Stomp and
attack him three times. Now pay
attention to the attack hints:

- If it starts to fly again (Sto
arena, avoid it and attack twice
or, if it tries to smash you in
other parts of the map, you can
attack three times, but in both
cases keep a medium distance or
you will get a hit from its next
attack in the middle of your
combo.

- When Fiersome returns to the c
head, showing a Fireball Vacuum
attack coming ahead. Go to the
left or right side (the one that
will give you more space to see
from where the fireballs comes),
pay attention to the fireballs
coming in your direction and try
to avoid them. You can hit it
twice after the vacuum stop, but
if you want to be safer, just
attack once.

- In the case of Fiersome raises
the Triple Fireball. Try to run
away from it to any side and
when you see all Fireballs, get
out of the way and run back to
Fiersome. You can also try to
avoid by other ways, you just
need to know that this attack
moves forward and turns 90 to
the side you try to avoid (an
"L" movement). You can hit it
twice if you are in a medium
distance.

- If you hear a scream after Fie
distance and keep watching the
Spin Attack, so you can keep a
safe distance from it (this is a
very slow movement). Try to run
horizontally to have more space.
Attack twice and run to the
other side (if it uses the Spin
attack again and you stay in the
same place, you won't have more
space to run, taking almost all
the hits).

Try to follow these hints until
Fiersome enters in Berserk Mode.
Now it'll have a new set of
attacks and some previous
attacks will be a little
different. Spin Attack will be
the same, so do the same as
before. Triple Fireball and
Fireball Vacuum will be no
longer used. Also try to kill it
as fast as you can, because some
attacks can be very dangerous
and difficult to avoid. Now I
will list the new attacks and
how to avoid them:

- The Stomp starts in the same w
pillars that rises from the
ground and moves away from
Fiersome. Run to a medium
distance and after you
understand the fire pattern,
just go through them and attack
twice (you can hit three times
if you are fast enough). BUT if
it flies to the center of the
map, don't attack and be ready
for Fireball Tornado Attack.

- Like Fireball Vacuum, the hint
Stomp at the center of map). The
deadliest attack, it will shots
two lines of fireballs, rotating
counterclockwise. Go to the
extreme southeast corner. You
can use Cure magic book or some
healing item if you get hit
during this time.

- If you see Fiersome doing the 
and no scream), try to move to
its side, so the Homing Fireball
will make a curve. Now keep
running in circles until it
stops following you.

Keep doing these tactics until
you finally kill it and enjoy
the first ending.


Green Underground Shrine Dungeon
Guardian - Greater Demon
--------------------------------
HP: 3200
Berserk Mode: 800 HP left
Attribute: -

Attack List:

- Impact: Close range attack. Th
 smash you, causing a little imp
- Triple Power Wave: Medium rang
 arm and hit the ground, shootin
 the shortsword skill). Medium t
 you take) and can cause stun.
- Rush: Used when it is far from
 run towards you. Medium to high
 take) and can cause stun.
- Stone Spike: Berserk Attack Ty
 activated at medium range and G
 stones spikes will come from th
 dodge and get hit by one of the
 Medium damage (one spike) and c

Strategy:

One of the easiest bosses, so
easy that is possible to kill it
without getting hit by a single
attack. Just get closer to it
and wait for an attack. If you
see the Greater Demon raising
its arm for Impact or Triple
Power Wave attacks, just run to
its side until you see it can't
hit you anymore and give an
incomplete combo of your
currently weapon (don't use the
last hit or you'll be open for a
second attack). If you see it
preparing a Rush attack, go as
far as you can, get out of the
way and get closer again and
repeat the same tactic. After it
enters in Berserk Mode, keep
doing the same tactic, the only
difference is that if you see
the Greater Demon raising its
right arm you'll need to keep
running on the map until you
dodge all the five spikes from
Stone Spike Attack, but don't
attack this time, just wait for
the next one.


Tropic Underground Shrine
Dungeon Guardian - Chimera
--------------------------------
HP: 3200
Berserk Mode: 800 HP
Attribute: -

Attack List:

- Bite: Chimera will shake its h
 direction and biting three time
 front paws and jumps even farth
 cause stun.
- Paralyze Blow: Chimera will ru
 will glow blue and then blow gr
 damage.
- Water Laser: Chimera will run,
 lasers into your direction with
- Scratch: Close range attack. S
 left arm and scratches. Medium 

Strategy:

This boss basically likes to use
counter attacks. If it tries to
attack first, it'll try to hit
using the Bite attack. So just
wait it prepares the attack and
move out of the way, going to
any side. Now try to attack it.
If Chimera just turns to your
direction, move to its side and
attack once (can attack twice if
you are fast enough). If it
starts to run away, follow it
and prepare yourself against a
counter attack. There are two
possible attacks that can come
now. If you see Chimera facing
you with blue eyes, dodge the
Paralyze blow by going to its
side and do an incomplete combo
(don't use the last hit or
you'll be open for a second
attack). If you see it giving
its back toward your direction,
keep running around it until you
see the first shot and attack
twice with a shortsword or once
with other weapon. In the case
you get a status ailment or need
to heal just go far from it,
dodge the bite attack and use
this time to cure yourself.
After it enters in Berserk Mode,
the Bite attack will be a little
different and Chimera will use
the Paralyze Blow and Water
Laser at will (not as a counter
anymore). For me the battle
become easier at this point
because I didn't need to pursuit
it anymore and had more time to
inflict more hits. Just do the
same as before (pay attention to
the attacks hints) until you
finally kill it.


Ravine Underground Shrine
Dungeon Guardian - Golum
--------------------------------
HP: 1800
Berserk Mode: 450 HP left
Attribute: -

Attack list:

- Double Punch: Quickly puts the
 careful, because this is a fast
 can cause stun.
- Rush: The boss goes down on kn
 rushes after you . Low to mediu
- Fireball: Golum moves its left
 magic level 3. Medium to high d
- Storm Punch: Berserk Attack Ty
 knees, lowers its shoulder, sho
 sides and its hands will start 
 direction. Medium damage and gi
- Rocket Punch: Berserk Attack T
 rockets in the shape of hands i
 and following you. Medium damag

Strategy:

A boring fight. Golum has a high
physical defense and its attacks
don't give too much time for
counter attacks, so I really
recommend you to use Magic
attacks. If you choose this way,
try to use multi-hit magics at
max level, like Sonic Wind,
Fireball, Water Laser, but I
really recommend to use Shine
(do the same strategy described
below, but use the magic instead
a physical attack). Get closer
to it so Golum will not use the
Fireball (but if you see it
using this attack, just run away
a little from it since the range
of the magic is short). If you
see the boss preparing a Double
Punch, avoid it by going to its
side and attack twice with
shortsword (once with other
weapons). If you see a Rush
attack, run as far as you can
since Golum can reach you really
quickly (it can rush from one
wall to another of the map) and
attack twice (sometimes you can
attack three times) in its back
when Golum is stopping. Avoid to
fight near the walls, as you
can't dodge very well from its
attack. If you get hit, try to
go away from it and get healed
as soon as you can. Keep doing
this until it enters Berserk
Mode. Now two new attack will
come and only fireball attack
will remain from previous set of
moves. If you see Golum raising
its hand, keep moving around
until all hands disappears and
wait for the next attack. If it
tries to hit you with the Storm
Punch attack, wait until it
completely stop and attack three
times (attack twice if you reach
it too late). Just do it until
you see its end.


Iceberg Underground Shrine
Dungeon Guardian - Grimoire
--------------------------------
HP: 3500 Berserk Mode: 900 HP
left Attribute: Wind (Use earth
type attacks for extra damage)

Attack List:

- Tail Sweep: The boss opens its
 hitting you with its tail. High
- Stomp: Grimoire starts to fly,
 High damage.
- Gust: Start to move its wings 
 and hitting some times. Low dam
- Sonic Wind: Berserk Attack Typ
 Sonic Wind spells that keep fol
 attack, it moves in small turns

Strategy:

Spears can be a good choice in
this battle, but as always, a
shortsword can do a fine job
either. Try to lure the Grimoire
to the center of the map (since
it's easier to hit and avoid its
attack) when you see it flying
to perform the Stomp Attack,
attack twice. If you see
Grimoire moving its body to
left, move away to avoid the
Tail Sweep, go to its back and
do an incomplete combo (don't
use the last hit or you'll be
open for a second attack). If
you see it performing the Gust
attack, simply get out of the
way and attack it from its side
or back with long range attacks
(that's why I said that spears
are a good choice for this
battle), don't get too near of
Grimoire or you'll be push back
with its Gust. When you finally
do enough damage and it enters
in Berserk Mode just keep the
same strategy as before. The
difference now is that Grimoire
doesn't use Gust anymore, using
the Sonic Wind instead. If you
see it raising its body, three
wind razors will try to hit you.
Avoid the first move and hit it
twice. Now keep moving and in
the map to avoid the razors and
dodge the other moves. Keep
attacking the same way as before
(but now pay extra attention to
the razors).


################################
9. Dungeons [Dungeons1]
################################

In this section you'll know more
about each of the dungeons
available in this game. I'll
give a brief description about
each of them and list the
monsters and what you can get
from them. The dungeons are
ordered by the season order from
the game.

After the general info about the
dungeon, the Details for Area
subsection presents everything
there is in each of the areas of
the dungeon that could be
interesting to know.

Each dungeon has an ASCII map
that can help you to identify
the areas of the map. This can
be useful for reference for the
the quests of the villagers.

Unlike the first Rune Factory
game, in this one all of the
dungeons are opened and can be
accessed since the beginning of
the game. All of them starts
with weak monsters (even though
some are easier than others, see
the difficulty level of each one
in their sections below). During
the first generation of the
game, you'll see a lot of paths
will be blocked by fences and
statues. Well, you can't really
get past these for now, that
will only be possible after you
have your children and start
playing the second generation,
so that means the possibilities
are very limited in the
beginning of the game.

There are 4 dungeons in this
game, and each one provides a
fixed season during the whole
year, so you can use the soil in
them to plant crops that aren't
allowed to be planted in your
farm when your not in the
correct season for the crop.

One thing you should know about
the soil in the dungeons is that
sometimes you'll see a purple
round mark in one or more of the
farming squares. If you do see
one, don't step on it! As you'll
be poisoned if you walk on it.
This venom won't go out by
itself, so, if you want to get
rid of it, you'll need to buy a
Neutral Agent from Natalie in
the village clinic and toss it
on the poison. By doing that,
you'll vanish it for good and
you'll be able to plant seeds
there again, if you want.

Another interesting thing to
notice is that when you walk
around in any of dungeons,
sometimes you'll find some white
flowers growing on the ground
(not on farming soil). If you
cut these flowers, either by
using the sickle or a sword or
whatever, they'll drop a rune
orb. These work the same way as
the orbs generated by fully
grown crops, except that theses
ones are less effective, that
is, they'll restore only a small
amount of RP when you pick them.
Either way they can be useful,
so make sure to collect them
every time you see one and your
RP bar is not full. The flowers
grow once a day and don't regrow
by just changing screens, so if
you already cut it one day
you'll have to wait until the
next day.

# Means Fences
& Means Statues

################################
10. Dungeons - Second Generation
    [Dungeons2]
################################

In the second generation your
character will mention that
grownups are too big to get
through the fences, but you can
get through, so you will have
access to different maps in
dungeons. Some paths are blocked
by strange statues and Kyle
couldn't do nothing about this,
but his child can read it and
get a hint as how to remove the
statue from the way, so just do
what it wants and you'll be able
to pass freely in the way behind
it. Also you'll be rewarded with
a Stone Tablet Fragment. The
Details for Area section will
say what you need to deliver or
do and open your path.

After you defeat Fiersome at
Palermo Shrine, slabs at all
Underground Shrine Entrances
(the room behind the last statue
of each dungeon) will be active,
so you will have access to the
secret seasonal rooms and bosses
(you can't take a monster with
you in these places). All of
them have nine room and, in
order to go to the next one you
need to destroy all monsters in
the previous room (they can't be
tamed) and also destroy the Gate
that summons them.

After defeating them, two slabs
will appear, one of them will
restore all of your HP and RP,
while the other one will do
nothing. The time will be
completely frozen, so this can
be a good place to train your
level and skills (plus you can
fight against all bosses again
after you do the second ending,
except Fiersome). Since the
first screen just shows your
currently room, there is no map
available for these rooms.

# Means Fences
& Means Statues
+ Means Door

access to it you need first
collect all Tablet fragments
from all four seasons dungeons
(five Green Tablet fragments
from Trieste Forest, seven Blue
Tablet fragments from Blessia
Island, five Red Tablet
fragments from Messhina Valley
and five Ice Tablet fragments
from Padova Mountains), check
each dungeon section to know how
to obtain them. After that talk
to Barrett (he won't talk about
the tablets in all locations) to
learn about this place. Get the
Dragon Break magic book from
Alvarna Academy - Library at
upper left shelf. Finally, talk
to mayor Byron and ask to him to
improve one more floor on your
barn (it will have no costs to
you and the expansion will be
completed just after you talk to
him, but first you need to do
all barn's expansions). Enter in
the barn, walk to the elevator,
select "Go to a deeper floor"
until you see the option
"Basement Floor 28" and choose
it. You'll see a giant hole on
the floor, this is the entrance
to Palermo Shrine. Also note the
after you had entered at least
once this place, you can bring a
monster with you by taking it
out and moving to the barn's
door. Two options will appear
and you can go inside by
selecting "Go."


Season: Your current season
(except in the 4 Seasons Hallway
floor) Danger Level: Not
specified, but no doubt it is
max.

Monsters you can find (Monster
drop in parenthesis)
--------------------------------
Anytime: Aerian (Magic Crystal),
Arch Demon (Devil Blood), Claw
Dragon (Rage Fang), Dark Faerie
(Fairy Dust), Demon (Devil
Horn), Faust (Hood), Gigantus
(Giant's Gloves), Goblin (Proof
of Warrior), Goblin Archer
(Cheap Bandage), Goblin Gangster
(Skull), Goblin Pirate (Quality
Cloth), King Minotauros (Hammer
Piece), Little Emperor (Magic
Powder), Little Golem (Bronze),
Mimic (Broken Box), Minotauros
(Hammer Piece), Monster Box
(Broken Box), Ogre Viking
(Glue), Orc (Cheap cloth), Orc
Archer (Arrowhead), Orc Viking
(Shoulder Piece), Titan (Giant's
Fingernail)


Items you can pick: -

Mining ores: Bronze, Earth
Crystal, Fire Crystal, Gold,
Iron, Platinum, Scrap
    Iron, Silver, Water Crystal,

Fishes: -

Search: Amethyst, Antidote Herb,
Aquamarine, Black Grass, Carrot,
Corn,
    Cucumber, Diamond, Emerald, 
    Gold Turnip, Green Pepper, H
    Orange Grass, Pink Melon, Pi
    Silk Cloth, Tomato, White Ca

Orbs:
- Spring Orb: Sow Cabbage and To
- Summer Orb: Sow Cucumber and E
- Fall Orb: Sow Carrot and Yam a
- Winter Orb: Sow Turnip and Whi
Note: They must all be fully
grown.


How to unlock all the rooms
(quickest way):

As you could see in the maps,
some rooms are blocked by
enormous doors. To get access to
all them and don't lose time, do
the following: First of all
bring your farming tools (axe,
hammer, hoe and waterpot) and
these seeds (one bag each):
Cabbage, Toyherb (Spring),
Cucumber, Eggplant (Summer),
Carrot, Yam (Fall), Turnip and
White Cabbage (Winter). You can
bring some Fur Sleeping Bags,
Formulas and Neutral Agents
(maybe you need this) if you
want.

From Palermo Shrine Entrance, go
to the north room (B1F Great
Hall) and try to run through the
north exit. Your character will
notice the two slabs (used to
unlock the door at B1F North
Room). After this go to the east
room (B1F East Room) and go down
one floor, move to north (B2F
Room 6) and active the switch.
Run one room to northwest (B2F
Room 4) and another to west (B2F
Room 5), kill everything and
activate the switch (the time
will freeze until you check the
statue, the same will happen in
others rooms with this trap).
Return to the last room (B2F
Room 4), go up one floor (B1F
Great Hall), move to west (B1F
West Room) and go down again
(B2F Room 1). Run to north (B2F
Room 2), activate the switch and
go to the southeast exit (B2F
Room 3). Go down (B3F Room 1),
run one room to east (B3F Room
2), one room to north (B3F Room
5) and one room to east (B3F
Room 7). Kill all monsters and
active the switch. Go back to
B3F Room 2, but now go one room
to east (B3F Room 3) and another
to north (B3F Room 4). Again,
kill everything and active
another switch. Now try to go to
B3F Room 2 (you need to kill all
monster in B3F Room 3 to keep
going), move two rooms to north
(B3F Room 8), kill everyone as
always and check the slab. Go
back to B1F Great Hall (use the
Escape magic book or just run to
there), move down one floor by
B1F East Room, run two maps to
north (B2F Room 8) and go down
(Mini Garden). Now you need to
pass through eight rooms (in
each room you need to destroy
all the things to keep going),
so it's a good idea to save if
you're not strong enough. Now
proceed until the last room and
active the slab. Go to B1F Great
Hall (use the Escape magic book
or just run to there), move to
north (B1F North Room) and go
down one floor (4 Seasons
Hallway). In this floor there
are four rooms in each extremity
(north way is blocked), so go to
all them, kill all the enemies
in the map, check the statue and
plant the crops that it says.
After all crops are fully grown,
check the statues and get the
Seasonal Orbs, opening the last
door.

################################
11. Advancing to the Second
    Generation [Second]
################################

This section will cover the
basics about what you should do
to proceed to the second
generation of the game and tell
briefly what changes and what
does not. Notice the times I say
will be fastest ones to start
the new events (have a baby,
build the school, etc.), but it
doesn't mean you need to do this
exactly in this day. Actually
you can activate these events
anytime from the day I say, so,
if you're not in a hurry or want
to delay the events a little
longer, there's absolutely no
problem about it.


********************************
11.1. How to Advance [Advance]
********************************

First of all, for the ones who
are not aware, the second
generation covers the story of
the main character's son or
daughter (your choice). So, if
you want to advance to this part
of the game, the first thing you
need to do is to court the girl
you like until her love level
reaches 10 and then marry her
(see the Bachelorettes section
to know about proposal).

After you marry the girl, wait 9
days (you don't need to give
gifts or talk to her if you
don't want...even though that
would make you a very bad
husband...) and then talk to
her. She'll then say she'll be
having a baby soon, and you'll
be asked to choose if you'd
prefer a boy, a girl or if
either is fine. Notice this
choice will determine the
character you'll be playing with
in the second generation, so
pick the choice you like the
most. I don't think there's any
difference if you are a boy or a
girl, except that you'll be able
to have girlfriends or
boyfriends, respectively.

Wait more 6 days after choosing
the gender of the baby and then
go out of your house. When you
enter the house again you'll see
your wife will be holding the
newly born baby. In this same
day, you can already talk to
Byron when he's in his house to
discuss the building of a school
in the village and, if you have
100000G and 1000 pieces of wood,
you can talk to him again to ask
him to build the school.

The school will be built in the
Cherry Blossom Square and it'll
take 10 days to be ready. When
you go near the school after
it's finished you'll
automatically start some
conversations that will end up
starting the second generation
so, if you still don't want to
go to the second generation
after starting building the
school, be sure to don't go near
the door of the school in Cherry
Blossom Square after the 10 days
period. Because if you don't
actually pass in front of the
door the events won't start and
you'll be able to keep playing
in the first generation. The
same way, don't forget to go to
the school in Cherry Blossom
Square if you do want to proceed
to the second generation.

One thing you should pay
attention before starting the
events that will take you to the
second generation is the amount
of feed you have left in the
barn for your monsters. If you
don't want to lose friendship
points because of lack of feed,
you must be sure you have left
at least 33 feed FOR EACH
monster you have in the barn,
that is, if your barn is full
(you have 16 monsters), before
advancing to the next generation
you need to stock 33 * 16 = 528
feed in the barn in order to
guarantee that all of them will
have enough feed to eat during
the transition.

Just after you start the second
generation, a hurricane will hit
your farm, killing some of your
crops, just as an ordinary
hurricane would do. Actually,
there's a way to avoid the
disaster and save your crops. To
do so, just activate the events
to the second generation (go
near the school) after AM 12:00.
This way, after starting the
second generation, even though
you'll see the house shaking, if
you look at the weather icon,
you'll see it's not a storm, so
it won't affect your crops. Not
only that, notice as well that,
instead of starting playing in
the third day, you'll start the
game in the second day, meaning
you'll have one extra day. Well,
all of this seems very nice and
all and it really works MOST OF
THE TIME. Yes, I can't say why,
as I still don't understand it
myself, but sometimes, even if
you do activate the events after
AM 12:00 as I said, even though
you'll gain an extra day and
you'll see the weather icon
shows it not a storm, if you
actually go to a dungeon you
have planted anything in and see
your crops, sometimes they'll be
devastated the same way as if
they were hit by a hurricane.

In short, if you want to try to
save your crops from the
hurricane in the beginning of
the second generation, do the
following:
- Save your game before activati
- Activate the event (go near th
- Check your crops in the dungeo
 fine, otherwise reload your sav
 another time/day and see if you


********************************
11.2. What Changes (And What
      Doesn't) [Changes]
********************************

Starting a new life means you'll
have a lot of different things
to do, but not necessarily
you'll have lost all of your
efforts of the first generation.

First of all, I'll tell then
what you keep from the first
generation. Even though it may
not seem natural, all of the
physical status of the main
character will be kept, that is,
his level, status, skills and
alike. Also, you'll have all the
money and items he collected
(that is natural), plus your
father Kyle will give you a plot
item called Ancient Script. The
tamed monsters will like you the
same way (the Friendship level
won't drop).

Note about the tools: As I said,
you keep the items from the
first generation, including what
you gathered, the tools,
weapons...well, everything. But
when you start the second
generation, you won't have the
tools in your backpack from the
beginning, but don't worry. To
find them, check the chest in
your house (in the first floor,
the one that was never used for
anything) and you'll find the
tools. The problem is that a lot
of years without use caused them
to rust and they are not so good
anymore, that is, you can't
charge them anymore (if you
don't know what is charge, see
the Farming Tools section). If
you want to recover the tools to
their old selves or make them
even better than before, you
need to expand the school in the
second generation, building the
Workshop, that'll allow you to
start forging and upgrading the
tools and weapons (see the
Crafting section for details).

Finally, I'll tell about some
things that will change when you
start playing in the second
generation. The two main
differences I think you'll
notice are: the dungeons, that
are wider now, meaning some of
the fences won't block the way
anymore, because of your little
size, that allows you to pass
through holes adults can't, and
the monsters that are a lot
harder to deal with. And the
second difference is about the
villagers friendship towards
you, that will all be at level 0
(I can understand why everybody
doesn't like you yet, but how
come your own mother doesn't
like you as well??).

Well, one more interesting
difference I can point is the
new opening, starring the new
generation characters. I think
it's very nice, specially if
you're a bit tired of hearing
the same music and watching the
same movie over and over
(well...you'll eventually get
tired of watching this as well,
but at least it will pleasure
you a bit longer).

There are some other changes,
but I won't discuss about them.
Just to mention, I can say
you'll find new girls and boys
in the village to have as
girlfriends or boyfriends
(depending on what character you
chose), new abilities are
available, as you can cook,
forge, create accessories on
your own and I think you're life
will be slightly affected by the
school schedule.


################################
12. Miscellaneous
    [Miscellaneous]
################################

Here you'll find some general
info that I think does not fit
very well in the sections shown
before.


********************************
12.1. The Bottles [Bottles]
********************************

During the game, you'll receive
some empty bottles as rewards
from villagers after you have
completed some specific quests
from them.

These bottles allow you to fill
them with potions and alike that
can be later consumed to restore
HP, for example. If you still
cannot create your own pharmacy,
you can fill your bottles by
asking Natalie to make you some
potion. You just need to ask her
to create one and give her 3
Medicinal Herbs and 300G.

Below are the bottles available
and how you can get them:

Bottle 1: Reward from Natalie
after finishing the quest "I
Lost My
    Stethoscope"
Bottle 2: Reward from Byron
after finishing the quest
"Please Find Someone" Bottle 3:
Reward from Douglas after
finishing the quest "Let's Talk
about This
    Like Men"


********************************
12.2. Earthquakes [Earthquakes]
********************************

During the first generation of
the game, sometimes you'll just
wake up and feel an earthquake.
They are pre-programmed events
and occur once a season on a
specific date. See below when
it'll happen:

- Spring 18
- Summer 11
- Fall 4
- Winter 23

Notice you won't lose the day,
even though the game plays the
sleep song after the earthquake,
you'll still wake up on the same
day, so there's nothing to worry
about.


********************************
12.3. Sale Off Coupons [Coupons]
********************************

Once a season you'll receive in
your mailbox a letter telling
the shops are offering a
discount in their items in that
day. The amount off varies in
each season and are only
available on that specific day,
so you should plan ahead to take
full advantage of it (doesn't
apply to all items). See below
the days you'll receive the
letter and how much you'll be
able to save:

- Spring 15 (10% off)
- Summer 16 (30% off)
- Fall 14 (20% off)
- Winter 15 (40% off)


********************************
12.4. Full Set of Tools [Full
      Set]
********************************

It's one of the utensils you can
buy from Yue on Wednesdays to be
placed in the Workshop. It's a
very well known utensil among
the ones who are familiar with
harvest moon games as it
contains the "Makers" tools,
that are: the Mayonnaise Maker,
Cheese Maker, Yogurt Maker, Seed
Maker and Thread Maker. All of
them allow you to create more
useful / expensive items by
throwing specific raw materials
in it. Below I'll give a brief
explain about each of them:

- Mayonnaise Maker: Produces may
- Cheese Maker: Produces cheese 
- Yogurt Maker: Produces yogurt 
- Seed maker: Produces seed by t
 this one if you have an active 
- Thread Maker: Produces thread 


********************************
12.5. Endings                   
********************************

This game have one great change
in the story and two endings.
You need to meet some
requirements to achieve them and
it is possible to do all of them
in just one save file. These are
the requirements for each of
them:

- Advance to the second generati
- First Ending: Defeat Fiersome 
open the Palermo Shrine by
getting all Stone Tablets
fragments, Dragon Break magic
book and all Seasonal Orbs to
open the last door (check
Palermo Shrine section).
- Second Ending: Defeat all secr
dungeon, collecting all the
Ancient Tablets and then talk to
Barrett. He'll learn about the
Omni-Gate spell and hide it. Go
to the Alvarna Academy - Library
and get it.


################################
13. QuickLists [Quick]
################################

This sections contains some
lists that allows you to find
something quickly. Each
subsection covers something I
think it would be useful to read
occasionally while you play the
game, so these tables omit the
details and go directly to the
point. If you want more
information about anything you
should try to take a look at one
of the previous sections, in
which I tried to cover
everything in details.

The tables are always sorted by
the first column topic
(alphabetically), except for the
quests, that are sorted by
villager name and by order of
request.

      Generation [List-Quest2]

for the first generation above.

more familiar with the game and

section in this guide.

********************************
13.3. Monsters List [List-
      Monsters]
********************************

This list shows some information
about the monsters in the game.
In this table you'll find where
they live, what they can drop
when defeated, what the monster
can do to help in your farm
(either by working on it on
producing something), what's its
elemental attribute and its HP
at level 0.

The HP of the monsters increase
when you advance to the second
generation, the values presented
in this table show the amount of
HP they have when you face them
in the second generation, as
it's longest part of the game
and where you'll expend most of
your playing time (I think). So,
if you want to know how much HP
the monsters have in the first
generation part of the game,
take a look at the Monsters
section in this guide.

If you want to find an item by
drop name, I'd recommend taking
a look at the Alphabetical Item
List table.

(D) = Appears during day (N) =
Appears at night (A) = Appears
anytime (either day or night)

********************************
13.6. Alphabetical Item List
      [List-Alphabetical]
********************************

This table contains most of the
items you'll see in the game (at
least the ones I've seen so far)
and it tells you where you can
get this item.

I won't list quest items that
you just need to get it and
bring to the requester once,
since they can be found on the
Quest List in this same section
and I think it would just cause
this list to be harder to read
and they aren't that useful for
quick consultation.

* Second Generation only
(D) = Appears during day (N) =
Appears at night (A) = Appears
anytime (either day or night)
